Reichstag Fire: Van der Lubbe Sentenced to Death 86

Torgler Imprisoned for Three Years for Perjury

Others Declared Not Guilty

Leipzig - The verdict in the Reichstag fire case was announced at 9:07 this morning at the Supreme Court. The entire courtroom was silent. The presiding judge of the Fourth Criminal Senate, Pommer, read out the judgment: The defendant, Dutchman Van der Lubbe, was sentenced to death; the defendants Torgler and the three Bulgarian suspects were acquitted and released. Van der Lubbe remained motionless throughout, his expression unchanged while listening to the verdict. Only Torgler looked worried. When the judge read out the section of the judgment concerning the policies of the Communist Party, both Torgler and Dimitrov took notes. The audience listened to the verdict without reaction. The seats specially reserved for government officials by the court had long been vacant, but today a representative of Propaganda Minister Goebbels was present. In the spectator gallery were Dimitrov's mother and sister, and Torgler's wife, who were overjoyed and tearful upon hearing the acquittal. The pronouncement concluded at exactly 10:00, and the court adjourned. The defendants were escorted back to prison. The audience, crowding outside the door, all wanted to catch one last glimpse of the defendants' faces. (Havas Telegram, 23rd)

(Berlin) The Reichstag fire case, tried by the Supreme Court in Leipzig, has lasted for several months. The debate concluded on the 16th of this month, and on the 18th, the criminal court of the Supreme Court held a secret meeting to draft the judgment, which has now been announced today: The defendant, Dutchman Van der Lubbe, was sentenced to death; the others were declared not guilty. (Havas Telegram, 23rd)

(Berlin) One of the witnesses in the Reichstag fire case, a worker named Zanker, testified in court that he had met the three Bulgarian Communist defendants (Dimitrov, Popov, and Tanev) in Romania. Subsequent investigation revealed that the testimony was entirely false. Zanker has been sentenced to three years in prison and deprived of his civil rights for ten years for perjury. (Havas Telegram, 22nd)

Dutch Envoy Protests and Applies for Commutation 87

The Hague - The Dutch Ambassador to Germany has protested to the German government because Dutch Communist Van der Lubbe has been charged in the Reichstag fire case and sentenced to death. It is reported that the Dutch Ambassador has applied for a commutation because, at the time of the crime, the German government had not yet promulgated such severe criminal laws for this type of case. (Reuters Telegram, 23rd)

(Berlin) Van der Lubbe still has a chance to escape the death penalty, but at most President Hindenburg could pardon him and reduce the sentence to life imprisonment. (Reuters Telegram, 23rd)

Russia Sells Ancient Bible to Britain to Purchase Machinery 88

(London) The Russian government has agreed to use the 100,000 pounds paid by the United States for the fourth-century Codex Sinaiticus manuscript to purchase machinery in Britain. The ancient book has been purchased by the British Museum and will arrive in London on December 24th. After Christmas, it will be handed over to the museum by the Russian government and then put on public display. This volume is the world's largest Bible, made of vellum, with four lines per page. The Old Testament has 200 pages, with 40 pages missing, and the New Testament is complete, with 148 pages. Each page is 15 inches wide and 3 inches long. (Reuters Telegram, 22nd)

Asian Students' Congress Opens at the Pantheon in Rome 89

Six Hundred Representatives from Various Countries Attend

Mussolini Delivers Welcome Address

World Civilization Degenerating Due to the Poisonous Legacy of Capitalism

Hoping that Eastern and Western Nations Can Unite in Solidarity to Rescue It

Rome - The Asian Students' Congress opened today in the presence of Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. Six hundred representatives from countries such as China, Japan, India, Persia, Afghanistan, Siam, and Egypt attended. Mussolini delivered a welcome address, stating that the saying "East is East, and West is West, and never the twain shall meet" has no meaning in light of historical evidence. During the two great crises of the world, both relied on the cooperation of Rome and the East for rescue, thus turning danger into safety. Western capitalist civilization has destroyed the unity and harmony that once existed between East and West, a unity that is the cornerstone of our entire history and on which European civilization was built. Today, this unity must be restored and made universal, or it will perish. The belief that Europe and the East must stand in opposition to each other stems from a mindset held by certain parts of Europe that cannot or will not understand Asia. A civilization built on capitalism and liberalism, which views Asia merely as a market for its products, is doomed to destruction. This is a matter of great concern to countries that have been degenerated by the poisonous legacy of capitalism. This reaction has been expressed in the revolutionary faith of Italian Fascism, which is fighting against a soulless and thoughtless civilization. (Reuters Telegram, 22nd)

Rome - This morning, Asian students held a congress in the Caesar Hall of the Pantheon. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini attended and gave a speech, the final paragraph of which stated, "The ancient history of Rome has been as described earlier. Today, Rome and the Mediterranean are being revived through Fascism, and will reshape the world's solidarity. This is why the new Italy invites you to attend. World culture has faced two crises, bordering on collapse, and has been saved both times by the union of Rome and the East. World culture is now facing danger again. The existing systems and ideologies lack a soul and are merely obstacles to mankind. The Italians and Fascists commemorate the glory of the past and hope that the Eastern and Western nations will unite again to jointly rescue it." The Prime Minister's speech was translated into French and German. An Arab university student representative of the Asian students thanked the Italian Prime Minister in French. Finally, an Indian female student, dressed in a gorgeous costume, represented the Indian students in blessing the Italian Prime Minister and the Italian nation. (Havas Telegram, 22nd)

Empress of Japan Gives Birth to a Son 90

National Flag Displayed in Celebration

Naming Ceremony Scheduled

(Tokyo) Official announcement: The Empress gave birth to a son at 6:39 this morning. Mother and child are both doing well. (Reuters Telegram, 23rd)

(Tokyo) The Empress has already given birth to four daughters. This time, the birth of a Crown Prince has brought even greater joy to the entire nation, both government and people. After the Imperial Household Agency made the announcement, the news was quickly spread throughout the country via radio announcements, alarm bells, and news extras. Cheers of "Banzai!" resounded throughout the land, and national flags were displayed everywhere to express celebration. (Dentsu Telegram, 23rd)

(Tokyo) The Crown Prince's naming ceremony is scheduled for the morning of the 29th at the Imperial Palace. That morning, the "binding bath" ceremony will be held first, along with ancient rituals of reading books and twanging bows to ward off evil spirits. A section from the Nihon Shoki (Chronicles of Japan) will be chanted outside the bathhouse. At the same time, officials selected to twang the bows will repeatedly draw and release the bowstrings in harmony. The Grand Chamberlain Yuasa will then write the Crown Prince's name on six sheets of thin paper, which will be presented to the Crown Prince by the Chamberlain, the Grand Mistress of the Empress's Household, Takeya, and the head female attendant. Meanwhile, the naming will be reported to the gods at the Imperial Sanctuary and the Imperial Mausoleum. (Dentsu Telegram, 23rd)

The World Rejects Japanese Goods 93

Japanese Finance Minister Advocates Granting Broad Authority to the Government

Implement Trade Management and Retaliatory Tariffs to Counteract

(Tokyo) In order to counter the exclusionary trade policies of various countries, the Ministry of Commerce and Industry and the Ministry of Finance, in consultation with the Trade Deliberation Council, are studying methods to improve trade management, tariff policy, and trade policy. Regarding this issue, Finance Minister Takahashi told reporters that the Japanese government should have broader dictatorial powers than foreign governments regarding trade management and retaliatory tariffs to deal with the ever-changing world economic situation. Tariff issues should be negotiated separately with each country to determine treaties. (Nichi-Ren Telegram, 23rd)

India Increases Tariffs on Sundry Goods 94

Japanese Merchants Anxiously Study Countermeasures

(Tokyo) The Indian Legislative Assembly has passed the tariff on sundry goods, causing great panic among Japanese merchants here. They gathered at the Textile Federation to discuss countermeasures and fear that this will revive disputes in the Japan-India Conference. Chairman Abe of the Federation said that it is India's freedom to change from ad valorem tariffs to specific tariffs, but the increase in the tariff rate by 100% will cause even greater losses to Japanese goods. The Indian side did not mention the new tariff rate to the Japanese delegation beforehand, and the Indian Commercial Commissioner Park also stated that tariffs would never be raised. This is a great lesson for the policy towards India. (Hua-Lian Telegram, 23rd)

France Abolishes Surcharges on British Imports 95

Surcharges on Chinese Goods Shipped to France are Particularly High

Should Request the Same Treatment

(Paris) France's abolition of surcharges on British imports is seen here as a major blow to the system of compensatory taxes levied on goods with devalued currencies. Although the French government is currently considering levying this type of surcharge on US goods as well, other countries that already levy it, such as Argentina, Canada, Mexico, Japan, Uruguay, and Paraguay, will apparently demand the same treatment as British goods. This type of surcharge was decided upon by the French government after Britain abandoned the gold standard in September 1931 to prevent dumping. Subsequently, the currencies of other countries followed Britain's lead and depreciated one after another, and the French government imposed surcharges on their goods one by one. A total of 24 places have been subject to this tax: Australia, Canada, Denmark, the Straits Settlements, Finland, Britain, India, Ireland, Japan, Mexico, Norway, Paraguay, Portugal, Argentina, Sweden, Uruguay, Ceylon, China, the Federated Malay States, Hong Kong, New Zealand, Soviet Russia, the Union of South Africa, and Estonia. The tax rate is generally 15%, but the rates for China, Japan, Hong Kong, and Soviet Russia are particularly high at 25%. Portuguese goods are taxed at 20%, and Canadian goods are the lowest at only 11%. However, currently, in addition to Britain, Finland, Norway, Portugal, Sweden, and Estonia have also abolished the surcharge because they have concluded new commercial treaties or new trade agreements with France that grant preferential treatment to certain French goods. As for Britain, preferential treatment is expected to be given to French agricultural products, with the exception of potatoes. As for the United States, although the French government has repeatedly considered levying surcharges on US goods since abandoning the gold standard, it has hesitated to implement this policy due to the war debt issue between France and the United States, not wanting to severely damage American sentiment. (National Telegram, 23rd)

Japanese Parliament Convened; Open Political Warfare Begins 96

This time, the question of a coalition between the two political parties and the people is present, and rural issues and other important topics are mounting. How political parties can use this issue to restore their credibility is the most interesting question. (Nichi-Ren Telegram, 23rd)

(Tokyo) After advocating the dissolution of political parties and leaving the Seiyukai, Yosuke Matsuoka set up an office in Marunouchi, Tokyo, and began operations. All those who share our principles and are concerned about the current state of the motherland, regardless of their class, are welcome to participate in cooperation and collaboration. Page 8

Bandit Suppression in Eastern Jiangxi Comes to an End 125

All Pseudo-Military Corps Were Defeated

Wu Qiwel's Troops Achieved the Greatest Merit

Nanchang Correspondence: Taking advantage of the Fujian Incident, the Red bandits in eastern Jiangxi advanced in three routes into eastern Jiangxi. Their collapse is described as follows:

Central Route 126

On the Central Route, the bandits were commanded by Peng Dehuai, with the Pseudo-3rd Army Corps as the main force, supplemented by parts of the Pseudo-5th and 7th Army Corps. Advancing westward from Lichuan, the Nationalist Army's Northern Route, consisting of the 58th Column and several divisions, took an offensive approach to suppression. They encountered the 4th, 5th, 6th divisions of the Pseudo-3rd Army Corps, the 13th division of the Pseudo-5th Army Corps, and the 54th division of the Pseudo-7th Army Corps in Tuan Village and Dongshan, southeast of Lichuan. Zhou, the commander of the column, led his troops in a fierce attack, penetrating into Baogai Peak in Tuan Village on the morning of the 12th. Approximately three or four Pseudo-divisions of bandits resisted stubbornly. The Sheng and Li regiments of the Nationalist Army charged in hand-to-hand combat, one after another, breaking through the bandit lines in a fierce battle until Shen hour (3-5 PM). By dusk, Commander Zhou, fearing the bandits' skill in night attacks, ordered the Xiong regiment to build fortifications on the heights of Cuodou Village to secure the position. The bandits indeed launched a dense charge at night. The Nationalist Army, resting and prepared, responded calmly. The bandits attacked several times, but all attempts failed. On the morning of the 13th, they retreated towards Xiong Village. On the 16th, the Nationalist Army recovered Xiong Village. The remnants of the bandits fled from Desheng Pass to Taining and Jianning. The Nationalist Army continued to pursue them, taking advantage of the victory to recapture Desheng Pass, a vital gateway from Jiangxi to Fujian. Commander Zhou telegraphed the victory to the Advanced Headquarters, declaring that Tuan Village and Xiong Village had been captured, with 500-600 bandits killed, 2,000 wounded, 500 rifles captured, and dozens of machine guns.

Western Route 127

The 4th Army, under Wu Qiwel, first occupied Chongren Wudu on the 9th. The bandits retreated slightly, ambushing themselves in the nearby mountains. Wu's army was preparing to build blockhouses when the bandit leader Lin Biao led the 1st and 2nd divisions (three regiments each) of the Pseudo-1st Army Corps and the 1st and 2nd Independent Regiments in a fierce attack on the Wu army's Shiqiankeng position on the morning of the 11th. The attack was fierce. Xiao Wen's regiment of the Wu army was responsible for the western defense. The outpost was thinly manned and was occupied by the bandits. The regimental adjutant, Huang Jingzhi, and battalion commander Chen Lü, fearlessly led two companies in a charge, recapturing the position. After repeated fierce bayonet battles, the enemy outnumbered them. The 2nd battalion of the regiment and Commander Xiao personally led special service company soldiers, adding reinforcements one after another, engaging the bandits in hand-to-hand combat, repeatedly charging until 4:00 PM, when all eight regiments of the bandits were routed by Wu's troops. On that day, Xiao's regiment, as a single force, fought against eight times its strength from morning to dusk. Falling one after another, they ultimately achieved victory, completely recapturing all positions and killing the commander of the Pseudo-2nd Division, Luo Bingnan (brother of the bandit army commander Luo Binghui; his head has been recovered and sent to the Advance Headquarters), as well as two bandit regimental commanders and over four hundred officers and soldiers. Bandit corpses littered the field. The remaining troops scattered and fled. Over a hundred rifles were seized (because Wu Qiwel ordered his officers and soldiers not to collect rifles or capture bandits, awaiting the clearing of the battlefield and joint requests for rewards with friendly forces). That evening, the bandits gathered their remaining forces and attacked all night, engaging in a fierce battle until the next morning. When the Nationalist Army's aircraft became active, Wu's troops still dispatched teams to attack, conducting a large-scale search of the mountainous forest. By the afternoon of the 12th, Wu's army had cleared the remaining bandits in the mountains, completely recovering all positions. The remnants of the bandits retreated to Donghuangpi. In this battle, the Xiao regiment's achievements were the greatest, and the sacrifices were also the greatest. Battalion commander Chen Lü, company commander Chen Zhanyuan, and five platoon leaders were killed in action. The entire army suffered over two hundred casualties. However, persisting for two days and achieving victory with fewer troops against greater numbers was a glorious achievement. Their valor was no less than that of the 34th Regiment of the 6th Division, which repelled the bandits in Lichuan two months prior.

Left Route 128

The commander of the Pseudo-Jiangxi-Fujian Military Region, Xiao Jinguang, entrenched himself in Zixi. He was attacked by Xing Zhennan's troops on the 13th for the entire day. On the morning of the 14th, Zixi city was completely recovered. Furthermore, the commander of the Pseudo-Jiangxi-Zhejiang-Fujian Military Region, Tang Zaigang, led his troops to attack Yujiang and Guixi, attempting to destroy the Jiangxi-Zhejiang Railway. They were also defeated by Li Yunheng's troops. The remnants of the bandits retreated to their old nest in Yiyang. The Advanced Headquarters received a telegram from Commander Li yesterday stating that the entire Pseudo-10th Army, combined with approximately 3,000 independent divisions from various places, attempted to cut off Jiangxi-Zhejiang transportation and harass Guixi and Yujiang. He immediately ordered Zhou's brigade to suppress them from the west of Guiqi's Silichiao bridge. They made contact near the west on the morning of the 11th. After a fierce battle lasting half a day, the bandits were ultimately defeated, with over 500 bandits killed and spoils of war being investigated. Observing the situation on these three routes, it can be seen that the bandits in Jiangxi are not far from their demise.

Guangdong, Guangxi, and Hunan Provinces Jointly Suppress Bandits 129

Results of He Jian's Meeting with Chen and Li

Changsha Communication: After the Fujian Incident occurred, He Jian personally went to Lechang last month to meet with Chen Jitang. In early this month, he personally went to Yongzhou to meet with Li Zongren of Guangxi to discuss the current situation and the issue of bandit suppression. All parties attach great importance to this, but He has not yet publicly expressed the results, so few people know about it. According to a military officer, He's trip had two major tasks: (1) Guangdong, Guangxi, and Hunan provinces decided to jointly suppress bandits. Because the Fujian side has reached a military agreement with the communists, the bandits in Jiangxi will have no worries about an eastern attack and will be supplied by the Fujian side. They will inevitably invade the Hundred Yues to the south or flee to the Three Xiang to the west. Moreover, the bandits are cunning, and there are fears that they will attack in the east and strike in the west. Therefore, it is necessary for the southwest armies to have practical contact and full preparation. Therefore, he went to Lechang last month to meet with Chen Jitang. In addition to agreeing on the attitude towards the Fujian Incident, he decided on specific measures for the southwest armies to jointly suppress bandits and provide mutual assistance. Also, because the actions of Li and Bai in Guangxi Province are of great importance, he met with Li in Yongzhou this month for two days of face-to-face talks. He argued that if Guangdong and Hunan provinces were to suffer from banditry, Guangxi would not be able to remain safe on its own and strongly urged the Guangxi army to assist in the suppression of bandits. Li agreed and established a joint defense and bandit suppression plan for Hunan, Guangdong, and Guangxi, consisting of seven articles. Guangxi Province is preparing two divisions of troops as a supplementary force for bandit suppression. If the communists attack Guangdong or Hunan, the Guangxi army will mobilize at any time, regardless of territorial boundaries, and provide mutual assistance. All joint defense and bandit suppression measures have been telegraphed to Chen in Guangdong for approval. (2) The southwest provinces will issue opinions on national salvation. Under the meeting of He and Li, Li stated that due to the national crisis, many of the central government's measures over the years have not been completed. He intends to put forward a number of specific opinions on the future national salvation policy and request the central government to adopt them so as to achieve sincere unity and overcome the national crisis together. He agreed and exchanged views. As a result, the generals of Guangdong, Guangxi, and Hunan provinces will formulate concrete opinions, solicit the consent of the Yunnan and Guizhou provinces, and then contribute them to the central authorities or the Fourth Plenary Session on behalf of the southwest provinces for adoption and implementation. It is reported that He himself believes that the results of his month-long efforts are extremely satisfactory and has stated to others that the Fujian Incident will not affect the bandit suppression. (December 21st)

Circumstances of Chen Jitang's Encounter in the Suburbs 130

Police Mistook Bandit Alert for Opening Fire

Chen Jitang Escaped Dangerously to Zengcheng

Other Tourists Suffered Instead

Guangzhou Communication: Luogang Cave in the suburbs is famous for its lychees and fruit trees. On the mountain is Luofeng Temple, also known as a scenic spot. Recently, with the opening of the road from the eastern suburbs of Guangzhou, passing through Longyandong and other places, one can directly reach Luogang Cave. In summer, the red lychees are abundant, and in winter, the plum blossoms are in full bloom, making it a particularly beautiful scene. Luogang Town has a light railway connecting to the Nanyang station of the Guangzhou-Kowloon railway. The plum blossoms along the way can be smelled ten miles away. Recently, due to the winter season, the plum blossoms in Luogang Cave are brilliant, and many people go to admire them. On the 17th of this month, Chen Jitang and his wife drove to visit. In the evening, the tourists returned one after another. Coincidentally, the locals in Lianhe Town near Luogang Cave have a custom of celebrating the "robbing of the new groom," setting off gongs and firecrackers. At that time, it was a time of heightened defense. The Panyu County Guard Team in the area was on duty. Chen was returning from his visit to Luogang, and the car he was riding in was speeding along. The Guard Team did not know in advance and ordered the car to stop. Chen's car did not respond. The Guard Team thought it was a bandit vehicle and immediately opened fire. However, there was a bodyguard vehicle in front of Chen's car. The Guard Team's gunfire was concentrated on Chen's bodyguard car, like a string of beads. The bodyguards, surprised by the sudden gunfire, thought something unexpected had happened and quickly got out of the car and opened fire on the Guard Team. In the stalemate, Chen's car quickly turned back and drove straight to Zengcheng County, and telegraphed the provincial capital to investigate the truth. Only afterwards was it discovered that the Guard Team had made a mistake. However, they had already received quite a scare. On the morning of the 18th, Chen took a car back to Guangzhou, but on the afternoon of the 17th, in the incident where the police mistakenly opened fire, tourists on the road were killed and injured. When the Guard Team and Chen's bodyguards exchanged fire, a tourist car happened to arrive and was also hit by a volley of shots. There were two men and two women in the car. One man was Huang Dongsheng, and the other was Du Weiye (Chief Auditor of the Provincial Bank). The two women were both prostitutes. One of them, named Huang Yulan, was famous for her dancing and social skills. All the patrons and harlots came to admire the plum blossoms. Unexpectedly, extreme joy turned to sorrow, and they were caught in the midst of the incident. The car they were riding in was hit by more than ten bullets. Huang Dongsheng was wounded in the shoulder. Huang Yulan was hit by two bullets and bled profusely. Du Weiye was hit by a bullet in the back. The driver of the car was fortunate not to have been injured. Afterwards, they drove back to the suburbs and sent the injured to the Zhongshan University Hospital on Baizi Road for treatment. When they arrived at the hospital, the prostitute Huang Yulan had already died from her injuries. The two men were only slightly injured and the bullets had been removed, so their lives should not be in danger. (Evening of December 18th)

Hebei, Shandong, and Henan Provincial River Affairs Conference 131

Representatives from Hebei, Shandong, and Henan Gave Reports

Resolved to Request the Central Government to Allocate Funds for Dike Repairs

Jinan Communication: The third Hebei, Shandong, and Henan Provincial River Affairs Conference opened at 10:00 AM on the 20th in the Shandong River Affairs Bureau. Those present included Chen Ruzhen, Director of the Henan River Affairs Bureau, Feng Chunxi, Representative of the Hebei River Affairs Bureau, Zhu Mingzhuo, Representative of the Henan Provincial Government, Zhang Lianjia, Director of the Shandong River Affairs Bureau, and all staff of the Bureau. Zhang Shouqian, a representative of the Shandong Provincial Government, also participated, totaling over forty people. Zhang Lianjia presided over the meeting. After the formal opening, Chairman Zhang Lianjia reported, stating that the Yellow River runs through several provinces and has caused damage every year. This year, the breaches in several places are particularly severe, so we must find a way to manage it to fundamentally eliminate floods. Today, the directors of the River Affairs Bureaus of various provinces and representatives from all parties have traveled far to Jinan to attend the meeting. The significance is to discuss thorough solutions and jointly make suggestions to the central government to manage the Yellow River well and relieve the people's suffering. After the speech, Zhu Mingzhuo, the representative of the Henan Provincial Government, gave a speech, stating that dozens of counties in the three provinces depend on the river, and the area affected each year is extremely large. The meeting should decide on measures and submit a request to the central government for funding to manage it, and ensure that the measures decided are thoroughly implemented. Next, Chen Ruzhen, the Director of the Henan River Affairs Bureau, reported on the Yellow River water rise situation this summer. The water level at the Shaanxi Prefecture stations began to rise in mid-July and ordered all county magistrates along the river to defend the dikes, but they did not all arrive. By August, the water continued to rise, and the situation became more dangerous. Because public funds were difficult to raise, the work was very difficult. Therefore, the elements of river management are, first, funding, second, talent, and third, power. These three elements cannot be missing. Regarding the engineering aspect, although the breaches this year have been closed, if the dikes are not repaired, the danger will be even greater in the future, especially for the Zhengzhou Yellow River Railway Bridge. In the past, fearing that the flood would damage the bridge, the Pinghan Railway had thrown many stones to consolidate the bridge base, but it contained a great crisis, because the water must have a way out. If there is no way out, it will find a way out on the other side. Now, the stones thrown by the bridge block the water's outlet. The water is small now, so it can be tolerated, but during the flood season next year, it will definitely breach the north and south banks. This should be addressed urgently. Then, Zhang Shouqian from the Shandong Provincial Government made a speech. Finally, Zhang Lianjia replied. After the speech, a group photo was taken, and the meeting was adjourned. Also, the Hebei and Shandong River Affairs Bureaus both issued a written report at the general meeting on the 20th: (1) The report requested that disaster victims who were employed through public works still had no livelihood and that the dikes should be repaired. (2) The report on the progress of the breach closure in the northern section. Shandong Province also reported on the resolutions of the second three-province River Affairs Conference last year, reporting separately on those that have been completed, those that are being completed, and those that have not been completed due to various reasons.

At 9:00 AM on the 21st, the three-province River Affairs Conference continued to meet, still chaired by Zhang Lianjia, to discuss proposals. There were five proposals from Henan, five from Hebei, and one joint proposal from the three provinces to request the central government to allocate huge funds to repair the dikes of the three provinces, for a total of eleven. The meeting discussed each proposal one by one. There was no break at noon, and it was not completed until 2:00 PM, when the meeting was declared closed. Regarding the joint proposal of the three provinces, the original text is as follows: "Regarding the proposed matter, the dike lines of the three provinces of Henan, Hebei, and Shandong are thousands of miles long, guarding northern China and protecting the southeast, which is of great importance. However, they have been in disrepair for many years. The riverbed is silting higher and higher, and the dikes are becoming thinner and thinner. The dangerous situation is already precarious. After this year's floods in autumn, the water rushed and eroded, making the dikes even lower, resulting in many breaches. The shocking reality is a warning. If we do not seek immediate remedies and properly manage them, the damage will be terrible in the future. Rather than letting the lives and property of hundreds of millions of people sink into the aftermath of a breach and then spending huge sums to close it, it is safer to take precautions and repair it in advance. The pros and cons are obvious. Our responsibility is to speak out. We propose that the governments of the five provinces of Jiangsu, Anhui, Henan, Hebei, and Shandong forward a request to the central government to allocate huge funds to actively repair the dikes to maintain river defenses and protect the people's livelihood. Is this appropriate? Please decide." It was resolved that the River Affairs Bureaus of the three provinces should prepare a detailed plan with attached diagrams and send it to the conference for compilation and submission to the governments of the five provinces and the competent authorities for submission to the central government for prompt planning and implementation to eliminate floods and protect the people's livelihood.

After the three-province River Affairs Conference was closed, the representatives of the provinces decided to go to Wangjia Pear Orchard tomorrow (the 22nd) to visit the siphon siltation project built by the Department of Construction and various river works. (21st)

Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Fully Completed 132

Total Length of the Entire Line is 360 Kilometers

Construction Cost is Less Than Half of Other Roads

A Ceremony Will Be Held in Jinhua to Celebrate the Opening of Traffic

The Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway has been under construction since March of the 19th year and has now been completed in four years. In addition to the Jianglan section (Jiangbian to Lanxi), which opened to traffic on March 6th of the 21st year, the Jinyu section (Jinhua to Yushan) continued to be built in November of the 21st year and opened to traffic to Qu County in November of this year. The track was laid to Yushan on the 28th of the same month, completing the entire line. The Department of Construction has scheduled a ceremony to be held in Jinhua on the 28th of this month to celebrate the opening of traffic.

At the beginning of the construction of this road, the authorities were limited by financial resources and familiar with the economic situation in eastern Zhejiang. There was no large amount of transportation at present. After several studies, it was decided to adopt a light rail wide-gauge plan to save initial construction capital, and all designs were reserved for future improvements. The total length of the entire line is about 360 kilometers, and the construction cost is about 13 million yuan. The average cost per kilometer, including general affairs expenses, is about 36,000 yuan, which is less than half of that of other roads. This type of light rail railway is particularly suitable for the initial economic development needs of our country. Therefore, after the construction of this road, the Yupi Railway in Jiangxi, the Longzhang Railway in Fujian, the Tongbo Railway in Shanxi, and the Chengyu Railway in Sichuan all planned to imitate it. The completion of the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway is not only related to the transportation and prosperity of Zhejiang, but also to the future of our country's construction.

In recent years, the situation in Zhejiang Province has been relatively stable and construction has been progressing rapidly. Now, the Fujian Incident has suddenly broken out, attempting to invade Zhejiang, but the authorities are still carrying out construction, which shows that the defense of Zhejiang is consolidated and the desire for governance is particularly strong. The reporter has summarized the construction process and general situation of the line as follows, to commend the new construction project.

Construction Process 133

Zhejiang Province's initiative to build railways began in the sixteenth year of the Republic of China when Zhang Jingjiang governed Zhejiang. After Zhang left Zhejiang, the project was shelved. In the seventeenth year, Zhang focused on the Construction Committee and was ordered to govern Zhejiang again. He telegraphed Du Yuan to Zhejiang to re-survey the rough line of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway. This line starts from Zhakou in Hangzhou, follows the left bank of the Qiantang River, passes through Fuyang, Xianglu, Jiande, Lanxi, Qu County, and ends at Jiangshan, then extends to Yushan in Jiangxi. In June of the following year, the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Engineering Bureau was established, but there were no designated funds for construction. The authorities then proposed building the Xiaochang Highway on the right bank of the Qiantang River (Xiaoshan to Changshan). To implement the initial plan to connect with eastern Jiangxi, the northern section of the originally planned Xiaochang Road line was extended to the Xixing Riverbank on the opposite bank of Hangzhou as the starting point, passing through Xiaoshan, Zhuji, Yiwu, Jinhua, crossing the Jinhua River, changing to Tangxi to reach Longyou. From Longyou westward, because there are automobile roads between Quzhou, Changshan, and Yushan, and the mountains between Changshan and Yushan are stacked, for the sake of saving labor costs and business relations, a section of the Jiangzuo line is still adopted, from Qu County to Jiangshan, extending to Yushan. The entire road has a trunk line of 336 kilometers. There is also a branch line from Jinhua to Lanxi, which is about 24 kilometers long. Since the entire road does not start or end in Xiaochang, it is called the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway again.

Project Overview 134

After the route was determined, the groundbreaking ceremony was held on March 9th of the nineteenth year. The section from the riverbank to Lanxi was first divided into two main sections and six sub-sections, which were constructed simultaneously. Later, due to insufficient funding, the work was delayed. After May of the twentieth year, the provincial government signed a loan contract with four banks in Hangzhou, and the work proceeded smoothly. On June 1st, the railway was opened to Jianshan, and on July 1st, it was opened to Zhuji. The laying of the tracks began, and the projects were completed one after another, and stations were opened one by one. On March 6th of the twenty-first year, the Jianglan section was completed, and the entire section was opened to traffic. This section is 195 kilometers long. From the start of construction to completion, it took exactly two years, with a total construction cost of more than 6,939,500 yuan. Among them, the provincial government used provincial bonds as collateral to borrow and allocate 3.6 million yuan from four banks in Hangzhou: Bank of China, Zhejiang, Xingye, Zhejiang Local, and China Agricultural and Industrial Bank. More than 3,353,490 yuan was raised by the provincial government itself. There were still 120,000 yuan deducted from the additional loan from the bank for the construction of the Jinyu section. The construction cost of the Jinyu section is estimated to be more than 6,110,000 yuan. Among them, the foreign material costs are allocated from the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity of 200,000 pounds. The construction cost requires 3.56 million silver yuan. The provincial government will borrow another 2.5 million from the four banks in Hangzhou. The shortfall will be allocated from the remaining proceeds from the sale of the Hangzhou Power Plant. With the source of capital, it is divided into two main sections and eight sub-sections for construction. The entire section is 165 kilometers long and started successively between November and December of the twenty-first year. The Jinhua River Bridge project is the largest and started construction on December 20th ahead of schedule. By July and August of the twenty-third year, the laying of tracks began in sections, reaching Jiangshan in early October. Longyou was opened to traffic on the Double Tenth Festival, Qu County was opened to traffic on November 1st, and the laying of tracks reached Yushan on November 28th. The entire line was completed, and it took only one year from the start of construction to the present.

Stations on the Entire Line 135

There are a total of thirty-six stations on the entire line. Zhakou, Sanlangmiao, and Zaizhan stations are specially set up to facilitate the transportation of passengers and goods across the river and are limited to business operations only. Within the Jianglan section, there are Jingjiang, Jiangbian, Xiaoshan, Bailutang, Linpu, Jianshan, Meichi, Zhibu, Baimen, Zhuji, PaiTou, Anhua, Suxi, Yiwu, Yiting, Xiaoshun, Tangya, Jinhua, Zhuma Hall, and Lanxi, a total of twenty stations. Within the Jinyu section, there are Gufang, Tangxi, Huzhen, Longyou, Anren, Zhangshutan, Qu County, Jinjie, Houxijie, Jiangshan, He Cun, Xintangbian, Xiazhen, and Yushan, a total of fourteen stations. Currently, there are two direct passenger trains running daily on the Jianglan section, each round trip. There is one mixed train between Jiangbian and Jinhua, each round trip. A material train is temporarily used to transport passengers and goods between Jinhua and Qu County. After the entire line is opened to traffic on the 28th of this month, there will be two direct passenger trains between Jiangbian and Yushan daily, each round trip. There will be mixed trains running between Jiangbian and Jinhua, between Jinhua and Yushan, and between Jinhua and Lanxi, each round trip daily.

Scheduled Opening to Traffic 136

Now that the entire line has been completed, the Construction Department has scheduled the entire line opening ceremony to be held at 2:00 PM on the 28th in Jinhua. At the same time, an exhibition of local products along the line will also be held, collecting local products from counties along the line and displaying them in one hall to facilitate observation by people from all walks of life. Moreover, since eastern Zhejiang is an agricultural area and cattle are a powerful tool for farming in our country, bullfighting will be held in Jinhua, hoping to take this opportunity to awaken the people of Zhejiang to pay attention to raising cattle. The Construction Department has already invited people from all walks of life to attend the ceremony at that time. Guests must gather at the Sanlangmiao Station in Hangzhou at 7:00 AM on the 28th, cross the river to Jiangbian Station, and receive a commemorative medal for the opening of the entire line at the reception office. They can take the train with the medal. The special train will depart for Jinhua at 8:00 AM. After the ceremony in the afternoon, they will visit the Jinyu section along the line at 7:00 AM the next morning. Guests who participate in the opening ceremony and do not go to Yushan can take the special train back to Hangzhou that night. The special train will have meals and lunch at the Jinhua Railway Station. One side of the commemorative medal for the opening of the railway is cast with a portrait of Zhang Jingjiang, the founder of the railway, and the other side is cast with the locomotive first invented by Stephenson. At that time, the Railway Bureau will not only distribute commemorative medals to the guests but also present a commemorative issue for the engineering record and the opening to traffic, and a record of the scenery of eastern Zhejiang.

Inspection Notes on Jiangxi, Anhui, Hunan and Hubei by Our Newspaper's Special Correspondent Ren An 137

Miscellaneous Information After The Suppression in Southern Henan

According to communications from Jingfu, the border areas of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, such as Huangchuan, Guangshan, Gushi, Shangcheng, Huang'an, Macheng, Luotian, Lihuang (formerly the famous Red Area Jinjiazai), Huoshan, and Liu'an, have fertile land and abundant resources, and many are surrounded by mountains and valleys. There are many towns and mountain villages that are like enclaves, beyond the reach of military and political power. Wealthy families are often overbearing, and officials are corrupt. Loan and tenancy conditions are harsh, so the Red bandits were able to incite and agitate, leading to a prairie fire. Since the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, the above-mentioned areas have been either burned by the Red flames or plagued by bandit gangs in more than twenty counties. In the past, the National Army conducted four encirclement and suppression campaigns, but ultimately, the Red Areas were too deeply banditized and there was no way to deal with the aftermath. Encirclement in one area led to banditry in another, and the problem was never resolved. This summer, Liu Zhenhua, Chairman of Anhui and Commander-in-Chief of the three-province border area bandit suppression, stationed in Huangchuan and supervised the army in a fifth encirclement and suppression campaign. After several months, the Red bandits collapsed one after another. According to reports, Liu, learning from the past experience of recovering bandit areas and seeing them rise up again, blamed the failure on the inability to deal with the aftermath. He has a new village facility plan and has established a new village office in Huangchuan to actively implement it. The reporter had long heard of his name and believed that his work might be a key to fundamentally suppressing bandits. He then took a train north from Wuhan to inspect southern Henan.

This time, the express train I took was well-ordered. At the beginning of the journey, I saw many bodies of infants abandoned in the woods beside the road. Although some were placed in small coffins, they were not buried. Perhaps this was because the area was still within the city limits of Wuhan and the police might interfere, so they were abandoned and quickly fled, which cannot be determined. However, there were still corpses hanging on tree branches, which was puzzling. In short, whether abandoned by the roadside or hanging on tree branches, they both hindered the hygiene of nearby residents and exposed the dark side of urban crime, which could not help but make passers-by cover their noses and murmur their disapproval.

The train passed Wusheng Pass and entered the XinDian station of Henan Province. At that time, the moon was shining brightly in the sky, and Jigong Mountain stood tall to the east. Numerous snow-white Western-style houses were built on it, set off by the dark black mountains and forests. Under the moonlight, the roofs of the houses could be seen clearly. According to Luo Mingjun, a Kaifeng resident who had visited the mountain for leisure, the mountain is fourteen miles high from the station to the top. The scenery of forests and springs is unmatched anywhere else. Every summer, people flock to escape the heat, no less than the bustling scene on the Shanyin Road. In particular, foreigners doing business and missionary work in Henan, Shaanxi, and Hubei provinces often climb the mountain in the summer and return in the cool autumn, making it an annual trip. The top of the mountain is called "Jigongtou" (Rooster Head), and its shape is very similar to a rooster's head, hence the name of the mountain. Whenever the sound of the train is heard passing under the mountain, tourists always rush to climb "Jigongtou" to overlook the winding and galloping train, which looks like a swimming dragon, and all exclaim in admiration. During the era when the Northern Warlords were in power, important figures from the north and south also gathered on the mountain in the summer to hold meetings, build houses, and plant trees, competing to show off their wealth. There were more than 600 houses on the mountain, among which the villas of Wu Peifu, Sun Chuanfang, and Jin Yun'e were the most luxurious. Among the three villas, Jin's villa was the tallest, and the flowers and trees planted were the most numerous, reaching 20,000 plants. Jin once served as the military governor of Henan. During the Northern Expedition of the National Army, he intended to break away from the Beijing government and become independent, so he styled himself as the commander-in-chief of the Defense Army. He was then defeated by the Northwest Army. Tang Shengzhi's troops, the forward commander-in-chief of the Northern Expedition, later excavated countless treasures hidden in Jin's mansion on Jigong Mountain. It is known that the copper coins alone amounted to 750,000. Other details are unknown but it is easy to imagine. The mountain was not only a scenic spot for tourism but also held significant meaning in political substitutions. Compared with today's Mount Lu, it was almost more so. However, Mount Lu is becoming more prosperous day by day, while Jigong Mountain is only missed by a small number of people.

Wuxi

Banning Opium Leads to Murder 138

Shi Muru, a 27-year-old resident of No. 13 Dapi Lane, Dongmennei, Jiangyin, was quite wealthy. Because he was addicted to opium, he was often extorted by local ruffians. In anger, Shi came to the No. 31 Taiping Lane Hospital in Wuxi in the seventh month of the lunar calendar this year to quit opium. He agreed with Dr. Qian Zhongliang of the hospital to pay 226 yuan in silver for opium withdrawal, promising to completely quit the addiction within a month. Unexpectedly, after a month, he still had not quit. Recently, after Qian Zhongliang injected morphine into Shi, he suffered from alternating chills and fever, and his condition worsened. He died the day before yesterday. Qian knew that he had caused trouble and immediately hired a gasoline boat to send the body to Jiangyin. Shi's wife, Sun, saw it and was shocked. Yesterday, she came to Wuxi with her relative Gao Huaide to negotiate with the hospital. Unexpectedly, Qian Zhongliang had long since disappeared, and the hospital had also stopped treating patients. It is unknown how this murder caused by opium withdrawal will be resolved.

Implementing the Widening of Nandiaoqiao Street 139

The section from Nandiaoqiao to Daigouqiao is an important passage between the city and the countryside, but the streets are narrow, and the houses are close together. Vehicles and sedan chairs often overturn. County Magistrate Yan ordered the technical director Zhang Dezai to design the widening, which is scheduled to be implemented on January 1st, starting with the demolition. In recent days, the city engineering office has sent personnel to survey and set up central stakes, and together with the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau, they have earnestly persuaded the residents in the area. Except for Jiang Zheqing, a resident of Daigouqiao, who has filed another appeal with the Construction Department, the remaining residents, Yao Zhiding, Ji Jinchu, Ji Rongchu, Qian Zishao, etc., have voluntarily demolished their houses in the past two days.

The main criminals, Dai Zongxuan and others, totaling thirteen people, have been arrested by the provincial government. The remaining fugitives, Huang Zixi and others, totaling more than thirty people, have also been wanted by the provincial government. It is now learned that Wang Lan, the Standing Committee member of the local post-disaster committee, Yang Airen, the Standing Committee member of the county party headquarters, and the family members of the victims, Du Xiangxing, Chen Fengren, E Zhensheng, Liu Yulin, He Yuqing, Zhang Yuanqiao, and Zhang Zicheng, came to the province this morning to submit official documents, stating the pain and suffering of the family members of the victims to the provincial government, and begging for prompt and generous compensation, while requesting that the arrested main criminals be severely punished to serve as a warning.

Yangzhou

Robbery and Assault at Majiazhuang 142

At dawn the other day, seven people holding wooden sticks and single-edged knives suddenly came to the home of Xu Chunshan, a resident of Majiazhuang, Yiling Sixth Township, Sixth District of the county. They also ransacked the house at will. After checking, in addition to the loss of clothes and valuables, forty-four silver dollars stored in the box were also taken away. Apprentice Tragically Killed 147

A certain Ji, who opened a sesame cake shop in the southern part of Fanchuan Town in the seventh district of the county, did not engage in proper business and roamed around all day long. Last night, he returned drunk, took a knife to threaten his wife, demanding money. While they were arguing, the Zhang apprentice in the shop woke up from his dream and immediately got up to dissuade him. Ji casually slashed with a knife, wounding his face and then cutting open his head, killing him instantly. Unexpectedly, Ji knew that he had caused trouble and fled in fear of punishment.

Qingjiang

Dispute over Dams Between People of Huaiyin and Lianshui 148

Huaiyin County borders Lianshui to the east, and the Liutang River runs across the two counties. This autumn, the people of Lianshui County built an earthen dam on the Liutang River in their county, which was close to the border of Huaiyin. This made it difficult for the water upstream of Liutang to discharge downwards. If there was a flood year with a lot of water, the river would inevitably burst in the fifth district of Huaiyin, which would greatly affect the farmland in Huaiyin. At that time, the residents of the two counties almost had a fight. The Fifth District Chief of Huaiyin, Cao Shiwen, stopped it to prevent an accident. The incident was known to the Eleventh District Administrative Office, which ordered the governments of the two counties to investigate and reply. Unexpectedly, the facts were different and the problem could not be resolved. Yesterday, Commissioner Lu presented the replies from the two counties to the province for special review to prevent accidents and asked the province to send personnel to re-survey to resolve the problem as soon as possible.

Local News

Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi Went to Hangzhou Yesterday Afternoon 153

Accompanied by His Wife and Others, Will Return to Shanghai Today or Tomorrow

Said It Was Difficult to Agree to the Merchants' Request to Exempt Taxes on Flour

Consideration Still Being Given to Sorting Out Customs Duties, etc.

Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi took a train from Shanghai to Hangzhou at 3:15 PM yesterday to discuss important matters. He will return to Shanghai today or tomorrow. At 9:00 AM yesterday morning, Chen Guangfu, Chairman of the National Economic Council's Cotton Association, went to visit Kong to report on the progress of the work. At 10:00 AM, Kong met with reporters from various newspapers. The following is a record of his conversation:

Tax on Foreign Rice and Wheat 154

Kong expressed his rejection of the request from flour manufacturers in this city to exempt taxes on foreign wheat that had already been purchased, and stated his reasons as follows: Merchants and the public from all over the country have requested the central government to levy taxes on foreign rice and wheat to alleviate the rural decline. The Legislative Yuan also believes that food and people's livelihoods are deeply related, and for the sake of alleviating the rural economy, it passed the levy of tax rates on foreign rice and wheat on November 17 and implemented it on December 16. There is a month between them, so the flour merchants in this city have long known that the Ministry of Finance will levy this tax. Now the merchants are using the excuse that the Ministry of Finance has not officially announced the import tax on foreign rice and wheat, and are requesting a tax exemption on 75,000 tons of American wheat that they have already purchased. The reasons are not sufficient and it is impossible to approve them. As for saying that I summoned wheat and flour merchants to the Central Bank at 10:00 AM yesterday morning to discuss the issue of tax exemption on foreign wheat, that is not true. Perhaps the flour merchants intended to make a request to me, but it was not me who summoned them. Kong also said that the tax rates on foreign rice and wheat currently levied by the Ministry of Finance are only slightly less than half of the highest tax rate passed by the Legislative Yuan, which can take into account the difficulties of merchants and the people's food.

Sorting Out Customs Duties 155

When the reporter asked whether the Ministry of Finance would implement an increase in customs duties starting on New Year's Day next year, Kong replied that the Ministry of Finance intends to sort out customs duties, but sorting out customs duties does not necessarily mean increasing all customs duties. There are many items in customs duties, and some need to be increased, while many need to be reduced. We will consider them separately and in detail. There are not many days left until the end of the year, so the saying that it will be implemented on January 1st is absolutely not true, and it is not possible in terms of time.

Levying Inheritance Tax 156

Since the Ministry of Finance decided to levy inheritance tax, various newspapers have published opinions. On the whole, the opinions published are quite different from what the Ministry of Finance has decided. For example, the Shanghai banking community believes that after the inheritance tax is levied, investigations of foreign bank deposits and road deeds in the concessions will cause various difficulties. This is an overestimation. The procedures for the Ministry of Finance to levy inheritance tax are as follows: for example, if A has certain properties and several children, there must be relatives and clan elders presiding over the division of the inheritance after his death. At this time, the government will start to investigate the amount of his inheritance and levy taxes. It is expected that there will be no difficult problems. The tax rates and detailed rules are already being drafted.

Petition to Impose Anti-Dumping Duties on Foreign Iron 169

The selling price in Shanghai is still 70 to 80 yuan per ton. In addition, it is operated by Japanese capital, and the price of pig iron in the eastern provinces has no public market price. According to investigations, it is also sold for 40 to 50 yuan per ton. Therefore, it is still difficult to fully prove the dumping of foreign iron, etc. The Ministry has reviewed and found that the investigations of the association are all true. The request to impose anti-dumping duties on foreign iron is difficult to approve. You are hereby notified." Signed, Minister Kong Xiangxi.

Total Mobilization of All Cleaners

Garbage Trucks Parade with Slogans

The 12th Shanghai Sanitation Campaign will begin the day after tomorrow (the 25th). This sanitation campaign will pay special attention to cleaning and sweeping. All cleaners in the city will be fully mobilized, and there will be a parade of garbage trucks throughout the city. All schools, factories, shops, and households will be supervised and ordered to clean up by the Education, Social Affairs, Public Security, and Health Bureaus. The details are as follows:

Outline of the Plan 172

This sanitation campaign will focus on cleaning and sweeping, and it will be jointly organized by the Public Security and Health Bureaus to raise the general public's awareness of cleanliness. It will be carried out in two parts: publicity and a city-wide cleanup. (1) Publicity: A. Slogans: Print four types of sanitation slogans, 5,000 copies each, and post them throughout the city. B. Leaflets: Print 100,000 leaflets (text to be determined separately) to be distributed to the public throughout the city by police officers. C. Newspaper Advertisements: To promote it widely, place advertisements in major newspapers urging citizens to cooperate with the government to rectify cleanliness for one day. D. Parade: Garbage trucks with slogans will parade throughout the city. (2) City-Wide Cleanup: A. Cleanup: 1. All cleaners in the city will clear out all accumulated garbage within their respective sections. 2. Police officers will order all households to sweep up all indoor garbage and waste and clean up in front of their doors. 3. Responsible officials from the two bureaus will inspect each district and examine the diligence of each cleaner. B. 1. Instruct the district municipal committee offices and district health offices to organize sanitation campaigns. 2. Instruct all restaurants in the city to carry out a major cleanup and whitewash the walls. 3. Officially communicate with the Education and Social Affairs Bureaus to order all schools, factories, and shops to carry out a major cleanup. 4. The Public Security Bureau will notify all district offices to implement a major cleanup and assist in all matters related to the sanitation campaign. C. Date: Scheduled for the 25th of this month.

Letter to the Citizens 173

Dear Citizens, sanitation campaigns have been held in this city more than ten times. The goal of each campaign is to take this opportunity to unite all citizens to work together to do a good job of sanitation, which is related to our lives. In addition to making every effort to eliminate things that hinder sanitation in the negative aspects, the Health Bureau and the Public Security Bureau will do some things that cannot be done by individual efforts in the positive aspects. If we want to do everything well in matters that everyone has a direct relationship with sanitation in order to achieve perfect results, then everyone must work together to help. Therefore, the purpose of the sanitation campaign is to ask all citizens to pay attention to the following words: (1) Cleanliness is the foundation of sanitation. Individuals should strive for cleanliness in their living places, food, and clothing. Publicly, streets and public places should also strive for cleanliness. (2) Maintaining street cleanliness can enhance the beauty of the city and the health of citizens. How can streets be kept clean? It depends on everyone's maintenance. Everyone should abide by the rules and not throw garbage everywhere. Even a small piece of paper or fruit peel should not be thrown on the road. Everyone should not urinate or defecate or spit phlegm everywhere. This will make the roads clean. (3) The word "sanitation" is not exclusive to the bourgeoisie. Regardless of gender, age, wealth, or status, everyone can practice sanitation and has the responsibility to maintain it. Shanghai 12th Sanitation Campaign

Page 10

Japanese Side Refuses to Release Kim Seok 175

Legal Discussion Between Two Lawyers

According to the Xin Sheng She, Kim Seok, a Korean who has become a Chinese citizen, was arrested without cause by the Japanese consulate in collaboration with the French Central Police on the 22nd of November this year. After repeated presentations of nationality permits by family representatives such as Chen Yang, requests were made to the Japanese and French consulates for his release, but to no avail. The Shanghai Municipal Government formally protested. The Japanese consulate initially delayed its response, but recently replied, stating that the Japanese government does not recognize Kim Seok's Chinese citizenship. This statement is not only contradictory but also contrary to modern international legal principles. Lou Yunmei and Xu Jie, the lawyers handling the case, have refuted the fallacy. The family plans to petition the Municipal Government and the French Concession authorities again tomorrow. The details are as follows:

Japanese Consul Has Already Recognized 176

Lawyer Lou stated, "Kim Seok was naturalized as a Chinese citizen in the 18th year of the Republic of China, not only with a permit from the Chinese government but also with the tacit approval of the Japanese government. Kim Seok and his son were arrested by the Japanese consulate in Shanghai in December of last year, and they were released because Kim Seok and his son had become Chinese citizens, which drew the attention of the Chinese government, which rigorously negotiated for their freedom. If the Japanese consul had not recognized Kim Seok's naturalization as a Chinese citizen last year, on what grounds would he have agreed to the release? If the Japanese consulate did not recognize Kim Seok's change to Chinese citizenship from the beginning, why did it not raise a dispute over nationality during the Chinese government's negotiations last year? It was not until this year that this fallacy was issued, which is not worth refuting. Japan claims to be a civilized country and should not have such contradictory actions. Therefore, based on the facts, Kim Seok's nationality issue can be said to be undisputed. Furthermore, in terms of legal principles, Japan's nationality laws do not deny Koreans the right to relinquish their nationality. The argument that people are the private property of the state and are not allowed to leave their home country has long been abolished except in a few uncivilized countries. Therefore, at the 1930 Hague International Law Codification Conference, there was a resolution on the following principles regarding the loss of home country citizenship due to the acquisition of foreign citizenship due to differing opinions among countries: 'Anyone who acquires foreign nationality through naturalization should lose their original nationality.' Kim Seok's naturalization as a Chinese citizen began in the 18th year of the Republic of China, and he has lived in Shanghai, China, for five or six years. Even if there is a question of nationality, according to international legal principles, he should be subject to the laws of the country where he resides and cannot be arrested arbitrarily."

French Police Station Should Be Responsible 177

Although the French Concession in Shanghai has granted police power to the Central Police Station due to judicial agreements, the French Police Station is suspected of being hasty in not investigating the facts beforehand. Therefore, although the main body that harms Chinese sovereignty is the Japanese consulate, the French consul and the chief of the French police cannot escape responsibility. Article 7 of the agreement on the establishment of Chinese courts in the French Concession in Shanghai clearly stipulates that no offender may be transferred to a government office outside the Concession without first being tried by the competent court. The French Police Station's assistance to the Japanese consulate in arresting Kim Seok is a clear violation of the agreement by not following the above provisions. The agreement was negotiated by the French Minister to China and the Minister of Foreign Affairs of the Republic of China, and both China and France should abide by it. The French consul has ignored this, which is regrettable for the diplomatic relations between China and France. When the second agreement expires in the future, our government should pay attention to it. In the case of Kim Seok's arrest this time, the French consul did not make contact in advance, and the French Police Station did not know that he had been naturalized as a Chinese citizen (see the previous conversation between the French consul and the French Police Station with Lawyer Xu), resulting in an erroneous assistance. Considering the agreement, they should be held responsible, and after the family presented the nationality permit, the misunderstanding should have been clarified, and they should have been responsible for demanding the return, but they are still perfunctory. We may not be able to say that it is intentional, but it is suspected of being close to shirking responsibility. Therefore, although this matter is directly only a matter of Kim Seok's personal legal interests, the main focus is on the issue of our country's sovereignty and legal rights. Appeals from families and a small number of groups are minor and weak. It is hoped that the central authorities will rise up and fight for it.

There Is No Dual Nationality 178

According to Lawyer Xu, speaking to the Xin Sheng She reporter, Kim Seok has been naturalized as a Chinese citizen through legal procedures, and the Chinese government, in accordance with the Nationality Law, has also granted him Chinese nationality. The Japanese Consul General replied to the Municipal Government that Japanese law does not recognize Kim Seok as a Chinese citizen, but Chinese law has always confirmed that Kim Seok only has Chinese nationality and does not recognize the existence of his Japanese nationality or any nationality other than Chinese. The reporter asked about the solution to one person having dual nationality. Lawyer Xu replied that in international private law, the so-called one person having dual nationality does not mean that a country's law recognizes that he has its own nationality and also recognizes that he has foreign nationality, but it only means that comparing the nationality laws of the two countries, one person has two nationalities. Since Kim Seok has Chinese nationality, regardless of whether other countries recognize that he has other nationalities, according to Article 2 of the Chinese Law Application Regulations, "...but those who should be considered Chinese according to the Nationality Law, according to the provisions of Chinese law," even if Kim Seok is suspected of committing a crime, he should be tried under Chinese law. This solution is not only advocated by international private law scholars but is also the principle for resolving dual nationality conflicts. As for Japanese law still recognizing that Kim Seok has Japanese nationality, it is nothing more than because of the provisions of Article 24 of the Japanese Nationality Law: a man over the age of seventeen, even if there is a reason for losing his nationality, such as not being exempt from military service obligations, will still not be allowed to lose his Japanese nationality. However, the 1930 Hague International Law Codification Conference had a discussion room on dual nationality military service, and its first article stated, "A person with two or more nationalities, if his habitual residence is within the territory of one of the dependent countries, and is in fact most related to that country, may be exempt from military service in other dependent countries, and this exemption may be the reason for losing the nationality of other countries." Kim Seok has established residence in Chinese territory for many years, and in fact, he is of course related to China. Based on the principles of the Hague Convention, Kim Seok has of course been exempted from Japanese military service obligations and has lost his Japanese nationality and should be subject to Chinese law.

Tomorrow's Separate Actions 179

Postal Associations Urge Implementation of the Postal Stabilization Plan 182

The Postal Economic Crisis is Worsening Daily

Implementing the Postal Stabilization Plan is the Only Way to Save It

The postal associations proposed a plan to consolidate the postal base last year and held a large-scale postal promotion campaign. Through the mediation of various sectors of the city, a Postal Economic System Research Committee was established. After more than a year of effort by the committee, an implementation outline for the postal base consolidation plan was formulated in June of this year and submitted to the Executive Yuan, which instructed the Ministry of Transportation to implement it conscientiously. However, half a year has passed, and it has not yet been implemented, leading to a worsening postal economic crisis and the emergence of numerous dangers. Now, the Shanghai postal associations, concerned about the difficulties of the postal service, urgently hope that the plan will be implemented as soon as possible to save it. They sent telegrams to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Transportation yesterday to urge implementation. The content is recorded separately below.

Telegram to the Executive Yuan 183

To Wang Jingwei, President of the Executive Yuan, Nanjing: We have learned that the Postal Economic System Research Committee passed the implementation outline for the postal base consolidation plan on June 15 of this year and suggested that Your Yuan adopt and implement it. However, more than half a year has passed since the committee concluded its work. During this time, news of the implementation has been repeatedly rumored, but in reality, there has been no progress whatsoever. When the staff recalled the committee's passage of the plan's implementation outline, they believed that our past efforts would not be in vain, and the eagerness for improvement filled the entire country. Unexpectedly, although the plan has been officially promulgated, it has not yet been implemented, and the public is extremely confused. The postal economic crisis is now imminent, and the only way to save it is to implement the postal base consolidation plan proposed by the committee. The staff is eager to save the postal service and hereby telegraphically request Your Excellency to promptly order the Ministry of Transportation to implement the postal base consolidation plan in accordance with the implementation outline passed by the Postal Economic System Research Committee and approved by Your Yuan to save the postal service and satisfy the public's expectations. The telegram is sent with the utmost urgency and anticipation. Shanghai Postal Workers' Union and Shanghai Postal Employees' Union, respectfully.

Submission to the Ministry of Transportation 184

Regarding the matter of submission: We have learned that the postal economy is exhausted, and the danger is now fully exposed. The most urgent task is to vigorously implement austerity measures, especially focusing on the big picture. In recent times, the postal authorities have also paid attention to this and have repeatedly implemented measures to reduce staff and streamline administration to demonstrate austerity. However, these austerity measures have failed to address the root causes, so the results have been minimal. Moreover, the postal economy has not only failed to recover but has become increasingly strained. The reason for this is the various expenses incurred by setting up separate bureaus for savings and remittances and the unlimited subsidies for airlines. If the Savings and Remittances Bureau can be merged immediately and the aviation subsidies stopped, the postal bureau can save enough each year to compensate for the losses of the past few years and restore the postal service to its former prosperity. This is a fundamental remedy for the exhaustion of the postal economy. We hereby submit to Your Ministry again, requesting that the merger of the Savings and Remittances Bureau and the cessation of aviation subsidies be implemented quickly so that the remedial effect can be realized. Furthermore, the recent dispatch of personnel by Your Ministry to Europe to inspect the postal services of various countries is very expensive and is not necessary for the current situation of the postal service. We have already telegraphed Your Ministry on this matter. We hereby submit to Your Ministry again, requesting that you give it careful consideration and promptly withdraw the order. The submission is made with the utmost respect and anticipation. Accompanying the submission.

The Ministry of Finance Rejects the Municipal Chamber of Commerce's Request to Reduce Factory Taxes 187

Commercial Downturn is Due to the Impact of Economic Recession

Does Not Relate to the Unified Tax Rate

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously stated that excessive factory taxes hindered the promotion of national goods and telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, requesting approval to reduce factory taxes to reduce the cost of national goods. The Ministry of Finance has now replied as follows: "Received the submission. This case was previously submitted to the ministry by the Shanxi Provincial Federation of Commerce and has already been clearly instructed. It should be known that the unified tax rate for cotton yarn is only 2.75 yuan per 100 catties for undyed cotton yarn no more than 23 counts and 3.75 yuan per 100 catties for those exceeding 23 counts. Calculated at the current yarn price, it is about 4%, which cannot be considered too high. As for wheat flour, although a special tax of 10 cents is levied per bag, after deducting the subsidy, it is actually only 7 cents. Moreover, before the special tax was levied, wheat was subject to other taxes and levies. After the special tax on wheat flour was changed, the wheat tax was uniformly exempted, which avoids the abuses of overlapping and harsh levies along the way and is not considered to be an excessive tax rate. Also, the unified tax rate for matches has now been revised separately. Although the table has increased, the tax rate for sulfurized phosphorus matches is lighter than that for safety matches, which will not cause any difficulties in the future. Moreover, the unified tax is borne equally by both Chinese and foreign merchants. The manufacturers are only responsible for collecting and paying the tax, and the actual tax obligation is borne by the consumers. The claim that the business of various manufacturers is sluggish is due to the impact of the economic recession and has nothing to do with the unified tax rate. The request for a reduction is not approved. You should be informed of this." This reply.
