Two Railway Lines' Train Arrival and Departure Regulations: Bell-Ringing Method 190

To be Implemented Starting New Year's Day

The Jinghu and Huhangyong Railway Traffic Departments have now stipulated the bell-ringing method before the arrival and departure of trains at each station and will implement it from January 1 of the 23rd year (next year). Yesterday, a special notice was sent to the stationmasters and related personnel of the two railway lines, stating: "The bell-ringing method before the arrival and departure of trains at each station on the two railway lines has not been strictly regulated, causing the station staff to be unable to follow it and to ring the bell inconsistently. Ringing the bell is related to the service of passengers and staff. The Director of this office, in view of this, has specially formulated three articles for the bell-ringing method for each station on the two railway lines, which will be implemented from January 1 of the 23rd year. All previous bell-ringing methods at each station shall be abolished from the same date. A copy of the stipulated bell-ringing method is hereby sent to you for strict compliance." (1) Starting Departure Station: A. Passenger trains at the starting station two minutes before departure, ring the bell twice for up trains, and three times for down trains, five times, indicating that ticket sales have stopped. At the same time, those sending off passengers on the train must also disembark. (2) Terminal Station Arrival: A. After receiving the exit report of passenger trains, freight trains, or other trains from the neighboring station, ring the bell twice for up trains, and three times for down trains, ten times, and stop ringing. If stopped, ring continuously to indicate which track the train should enter. The number of rings should be the same as the number of the track. (The stationmaster and switchman must still exchange hand signals as required.) B. When passenger trains arrive at the two terminal stations of Shanghai and Nanjing, the bell ringers should be handled by the Shanghai and Nanjing flag wavers. (3) En Route Stop and Non-Stop Stations: A. After receiving the exit report of passenger trains, freight trains, or other trains from the neighboring station, regardless of whether the train is scheduled to stop at the station or not, or is stopping for a meeting, ring the bell twice for up trains, and three times for down trains, ten times, and stop ringing. After a short pause, ring continuously to indicate which track the train should enter. The number of rings should be the same as the number of the track. (The stationmaster and switchman must still exchange hand signals as required.) B. Two minutes before the departure of passenger trains between Zhenjiang, Changzhou, Wuxi, Suzhou, Songjiang, Jiaxing, Changan, Hangzhou, and Yuyao stations (according to the scheduled time for each train to enter the station, according to the actual time), ring the bell twice for up trains, and three times for down trains, three times, indicating that ticket sales have stopped. At the same time, those sending off passengers on the train must also disembark. C. When passenger trains arrive at other stations within the station outside of Station B, ring the bell twice for up trains, and three times for down trains, three times, indicating that ticket sales have stopped. If the train needs to remain at the station to wait for a meeting or there are other special circumstances, then extend the ticket sales time.

Robbery and Gunfight on Avenue Foch 196

Four Robbers Forcibly Rob a Milk Shop

Police Pursue and Encounter Resistance

Stray Bullets Wound Male and Female Pedestrians

Rickshaw Puller Dies from Gunshot Wound

At 6:45 PM last night, a robbery occurred on Rue Massenet, French Concession. While the robbers were fleeing after the public robbery, they were secretly followed by an employee of the victim's family, all the way to Avenue Foch near Rue Auguste Villeret. The employee reported to the Chinese and Vietnamese police. As the police were about to move forward to arrest them, the robbers noticed and first opened fire to resist arrest. As a result, they still escaped. Stray bullets killed a rickshaw puller and seriously injured a woman in the rickshaw. The details are recorded below.

Milk Shop Business Flourishes 197

No. 19, Nanshan Lane, Rue de Montauban, Rue Massenet, French Concession, is an old-fashioned bungalow, six large rooms facing north and south, with a large courtyard in the middle. Because the house is located at the end of the lane, it is extremely quiet. Chen Yicheng, a native of Pudong, established a milk shop there several years ago, named Kangti Milk Shop, with 19 Chinese and Western cows. It has more than 100 regular customers. The business has been quite prosperous. Chen, due to other business, handed over the shop to Jin Axi (also known as Jin Asan), a native of Luodian, to manage. In addition to the three rooms at the south end, which were converted into a cow shed, Jin's family lived in the three bungalows on the north side.

Two Robbers Enter the Bedroom Directly 198

At about 5:40 PM last night, Jin had just finished his work and returned home. He had just entered the bedroom, taken off his coat, and was talking to his relative, Wu, when suddenly five robbers burst in from the main gate. Three robbers were armed with pistols, and two robbers entered the bedroom directly, prohibiting them from making any noise. One robber immediately snatched a pair of gold earrings from Wu's ears and a gold ring from his left hand. Another robber searched Jin's body and stole 26 yuan in cash. The robbers, seeing that there was nothing else of value, fled out the door.

Four Police Officers Hear the News and Pursue 199

During the public robbery, a milk delivery employee of Jin, named Du Gendi, was very quick-witted. He hid in the corner of the room, quietly observing the situation. When he saw the robbers leave the door and flee, he secretly followed them, step by step, all the way to Avenue Foch near Rue Auguste Villeret, and urgently reported it to Vietnamese police officer No. 320 and No. 286, and Chinese police officers No. 471 and No. 467. The four police officers heard the news and rushed to intercept them.

Two Robbers Open Fire to Resist Arrest 200

As the four police officers were about to move forward, two of the robbers had already noticed and pulled out their guns to fire. The Vietnamese police officers also fired back with their rifles. However, that place was a thoroughfare between the Chinese and French territories, with heavy traffic and even more dense pedestrians. In a flash, they disappeared into the crowd and escaped without a trace. A Jiangyin woman, Zhu Leishi, 33 years old, who lived at No. 20, Runan Lane, Ximen Road, happened to be riding in a rickshaw to the home of her relative, Jin Yunlong, at No. 26, Tongkang Lane, Avenue Foch. Unexpectedly, she suffered as an innocent bystander.

A Stray Bullet Wounds a Pedestrian 201

When the two sides exchanged fire, a bullet happened to hit the chest of a rickshaw puller, piercing a hole through it, and reaching Madam Zhu Lei's buttocks. The rickshaw puller fell to the ground in response, and Madam Lei also fell from the rickshaw. Amidst the chaos, the French police had already heard the alarm and dispatched a large number of Chinese and Western detectives to encircle and capture [the shooters]. Seeing the rickshaw puller and Madam Lei lying at the doorway of Pan Changxing rickshaw shop at No. 324, they used a vehicle to send the rickshaw puller to the Jin Shenfu Road Guangci Hospital, and Madam Lei to Renji Hospital.

The Rickshaw Puller Dies Immediately from Severe Wounds 202

The rickshaw puller was sent to the hospital, but because the wound was in a vital area, he soon died. The police inspected the rickshaw, noting the numbers as 12161 in the French Concession and 632 in the Chinese area. They immediately notified the Rickshaw Office to determine the owner of the rickshaw, so that the surname of the deceased could be known. Meanwhile, the police notified the Tongren Fuyuan Funeral Home to transport the body to the coroner's office, pending a report to the Second Special District Court for examination.

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Will Exhibit Chinese Bookkeeping Methods This Afternoon 204

Forty-Three Types of Books, Ledgers, and Forms

A Public Lecture Will Be Held Starting at 4:00 PM

Xu Yongzuo, a Certified Public Accountant and accounting consultant to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, has made a great contribution to the accounting profession by improving Chinese bookkeeping methods. Since their publication, they have been greatly praised and widely adopted by the industrial, commercial, and business communities. In order to promote and introduce them, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce has scheduled to exhibit these improved bookkeeping methods starting at 2:00 PM this afternoon, allowing the public to view them. At 4:00 PM, Xu Yongzuo will be invited to give a lecture. It is certain to be a grand occasion. Details are as follows:

Types of Accounting Books 205

There are forty-three types of improved Chinese bookkeeping forms, the most important of which are the Journal, Subsidiary Journal, Notes Receivable Book, Goods Book, General Journal, Clean Copy Book, Double-Entry Balance Clean Copy Book, Single-Entry Balance Clean Copy Book, Alphabetical Clean Copy Book, Consignment Customer Ledger, Sales Customer Ledger, Fixtures Book, General Ledger, Stock Ledger, Four-Column Reconciliation Table, Receipts and Payments Reconciliation Table, Receipts and Payments Sequence Table, Inventory Check Table, Receipt Voucher, Payment Voucher, Transfer Voucher, etc. All the books are printed with high-quality domestic Haiyue paper. There are also many charts to illustrate the classification of accounts and the organization of accounting books.

Exhibition and Lecture 206

Starting at 2:00 PM this afternoon, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce will publicly exhibit the above-mentioned improved bookkeeping methods in the main meeting room on the second floor, with filled-in examples of their use for public viewing. The Xu CPA Firm will send several staff members to explain the usage and answer questions. At 4:00 PM, a lecture will be held in the conference hall, where Mr. Xu will personally give a lecture and distribute two types of printed materials. The chairman, Wang Xiaolai, will deliver an introductory speech. Anyone interested in studying these methods is welcome to attend.

Service Department Established 207

In order to promote this improved Chinese bookkeeping and serve society, Xu CPA Firm has established a service department at its office on the 5th floor of No. 38 Avenue Edward VII, effective immediately. The scope of services will temporarily include guidance and organization for the improvement of both Chinese and Western bookkeeping methods. All inquiries regarding the above-mentioned issues will be answered and guided in detail.

Continued Hearing Yesterday in the Zheng Tangsheng Kidnapping Case 208

Locals Zheng Tangsheng, Shang Zhen from Henan, and Liu Yimin and Li Shaoting from Yangzhou, along with accomplices who are still at large and Geng Huatang from Shandong, who died by hanging, kidnapped five people in Shanghai between the winter of 1930 and February of last year: Huang Yuyi, Chen Yanghe, He Shaoting, Gu Zelin, and Huang Baohua. They demanded huge ransoms for their release. They also strangled a fellow gang member, Xiao Shaoxing. In Tianjin, they kidnapped Chen Zhuling and Liang Huiwu, former compradors of Jardine Matheson, but failed to collect the ransom and killed them, burying their bodies to eliminate the evidence. Jin Jiulin, the chief inspector of the special unit of the French police, learned in July of this year that Zheng and the other bandits were hiding in Tianjin. He dispatched detective Zhang Ziying, deputy detectives Qian Yumin and Zhou Bingcheng, and other detectives to Tianjin, arrested Zheng, Shang, Liu, Li, and Geng, and escorted them back to Shanghai. They were handed over to the Second Special District Court for public prosecution. During the trial, Geng Huatang committed suicide in the police station's detention center out of fear of punishment. Zheng and Shang, who were in custody, heard the news of Geng's suicide and also desperately attempted to hang themselves at the same time, but they were discovered and rescued by the guards. After the trial concluded, Zheng, Shang, Liu, and Li were found guilty of repeated offenses of aiding in kidnapping for ransom and were sentenced to death, pending approval by the provincial government. Zheng and the others refused to accept this verdict and submitted a petition to the Jiangsu Provincial Government, requesting a retrial to clear their names. The provincial government approved the request and returned the case to the Second Special District Court. Wang Gangxu, the chief judge of the criminal court, opened the trial on the 8th of this month. All four defendants overturned their previous confessions and denied participating in the kidnappings. The judge noted that key witnesses, including the kidnapped victims and the police detectives who handled the case, had not been summoned for questioning, and ordered a postponement for further hearing. These details were reported in previous newspapers. Yesterday afternoon, the adjourned hearing took place. The defense attorneys hired by the defendants – Zhu Fojiu, Zhu Dianqing, Fan Gang, and Qian Shusheng – arrived at the court on time to await instructions. The police detectives Zhang Ziying, Qian Yumin, Zhou Bingcheng, and detectives Qin Youyu and Cui Zhenguo also reported their arrival to await questioning. However, the victims Chen Yanghe, Gu Zizhen, and Huang Baohua did not appear; only Huang Yuyi and He Shaoting sent their bodyguards, Ma Pingan, and chauffeur, Yu Yonghuai, as representatives. At 3:45 PM, Judge Wang, accompanied by clerk Ren, took his seat in the Second Criminal Court for the hearing. Lawyers Yao Zhaodi and Gu Shouxi appeared in court on behalf of the police. The judge ordered the bailiffs to bring the four defendants – Zheng, Shang, Liu, and Li – from the detention center for questioning. After a brief questioning, the judge called witness Ma Pingan to the stand, first ordering him to take an oath. Ma testified that he had been Huang Yuyi's bodyguard for five years. He said his master was in Xiamen, so he was sent as a representative today. On the day Huang was kidnapped, he was returning home in a car when a free car followed them. At the intersection of Avenue Foch and Great Western Road, the free car sped up and cut in front of them, blocking the road. Their car had to slow down. The kidnappers then came up. He and another bodyguard, surnamed Wu, got out of the car and opened fire to resist. Wu was shot dead, and he was wounded in his right palm and left leg. Because he had used all five bullets he carried, he was unable to do anything. His master was then kidnapped. The kidnappers had two pistols. They fired first, trying to kill them. The kidnappers fired more than thirty shots. He said he could still remember the faces of two of the kidnappers. The judge ordered him to identify whether any of the four defendants present were at the scene. Ma turned around and carefully examined Zheng and the others for a long time, and replied that he could not recognize any of them. While testifying, he also demonstrated how he resisted at the time. Then, Yu Yonghuai was called to the stand and ordered to take an oath. He was questioned about the kidnapping of He Shaoting. He testified that he had been He's driver for four or five years. At 9:45 AM on August 30 of last year, his master was in the car, and he was driving from Rue Cardinal Mercier eastward. When they reached the intersection of Route Doumer and wanted to turn, the car slowed down. At that time, two kidnappers rushed up, one wearing a long gown who took the wheel, and one wearing a Xiangyunsha shirt and pants who pressed him down. He was shot in the back with a pistol. Because he was terrified, he couldn't see the faces of the kidnappers. Several other kidnappers came up from behind, but he didn't know who they were. His master was then kidnapped. He said his master had been in Beiping for a long time, so he was sent as a representative today to testify. Then, detective Zhang Ziying was called to the stand and questioned about the case investigation. The judge said further investigation was needed and ordered a postponement for another hearing. The defendants were returned to the detention center.

Lu Yimin Impersonates a Lawyer 209

Lu Yimin, who claims to be a lawyer, organized the "Minquan Law Office" on Route Remi in the International Settlement, undertaking litigation and non-litigation matters. Recently, in a rental dispute between Qiao Fangxi and Zhao Weijiang, Lu Yimin sent a letter to lawyer Zhou Yingjie. After receiving the letter, Zhou Yingjie found that the letterhead bore the titles "Former Envoy of Pacification for the Army and Navy of Guangdong Public Mansion," "Former Acting President of the Supreme Court of the Provisional Government," "Former Pacification Envoy for Shandong, Henan, and Shanxi of the National Revolutionary Army," and "Doctor of Law, Attorney Lu Yimin." He checked the membership directory of the Shanghai Bar Association and found no Lu Yimin. He also inquired with the association, which confirmed that no such person existed. Lawyer Zhou believed that Lu was impersonating a lawyer and sent a letter to the standing committee of the Shanghai Bar Association, requesting them to investigate. After confirming the matter, they submitted a document to the chief prosecutor of the Shanghai First Special District Court, requesting an investigation and prosecution. After reviewing the document, the court has ordered the relevant police station to summon Lu for investigation and verification.

New Year's Day Women's Social Gathering and National Goods Parade

The National Goods Maintenance Association Appoints Three Commissioners to Preside Over Preparations

Letter to the Municipal Government 211

The New Year is approaching again, and we should continue our efforts to achieve the goal of national salvation through national goods. Inspector Zhang Shouts Down "Third Madam" 213

Zhao Wu, a Spiritual Medium, Brings Trouble

Zhao Wu, a female spiritual medium, is 44 years old and originally from Shanghai. She lives at No. 120 Dong Street, inside Xiaodongmen in Nanshi. Recently, she had another imaginative idea, setting up a private altar at home and claiming to be possessed by the "Third Madam," the wife of the "Third Lord" from Mount Shangfang. She specialized in interpreting incense sticks, treating illnesses, and predicting good and bad fortune for others. She also used incense ash as a fake elixir to collect money, and secretly had people spread rumors that the "Third Madam" had saved many poor people, cured many sick people, and that those who played the lottery and wanted to know which door would open that day could also go to make a vow and draw a lot, and that everything would be answered and unbelievably effective. As a result, many ignorant men and women and lottery gamblers flocked to her. Therefore, her daily income was very large. However, yesterday, Patrol Inspector Zhang Panchi of the Second Precinct of the First District heard about this and, believing that she was using superstitious talk to mislead the public and extort money, violating the ban, rushed to her address around noon and arrested her. He brought her and the bamboo sticks used for drawing lots back to the station, where Police Chief Liu conducted a preliminary interrogation and ordered her detention pending investigation. Unexpectedly, after Zhao Wu was detained in the detention center, she suddenly started hissing and shut her eyes tightly, flailing her arms and legs, claiming that the Third Madam had descended. "You arrested me here, let me tell you, you can't scare me away," she said, putting on an act and making ugly faces, trying to convince the station that the Third Madam was not fake and they wouldn't dare to make things difficult for her. When Inspector Zhang saw this, he was furious and stepped forward and shouted at her. The woman immediately opened her eyes and was as still as a wooden chicken. Inspector Zhang then jokingly said, "You said the Third Madam was bold and couldn't be scared away, so why did she return to her Shangfang Mountain as soon as I shouted?" At this point, the woman knew her tricks had failed, lowered her head, and said nothing. Inspector Zhang laughed it off.

The First Scholarship Awards of the Beiping People's Review Society Are Announced 214

Total Prize Money of Two Hundred Yuan

The Beiping People's Review Society, publisher of the People's Review, has been in publication for two years. Seven winners were selected for the third topic, "My School Life," and the fourth topic, "Creative Fiction": Qi Peirong (Beiping High School), receiving a prize of 20 yuan; Zhang Bingxin (Northeast University), Liu Zengxiu (Beiping High School), Wang Sishen (China University), Song Zhibin (Beiping High School), Wang Yifa (Beiping YMCA English School), and Liu Yingxiang (unknown), each receiving 10 yuan. Historical Evaluation of the Leadership System" and "What China Needs Now" and "2. The Battle of the Great Wall" (creative fiction), will close at the end of January next year.

Fire in the City Yesterday Morning 216

More Than Ten Houses Burned Down, Affecting More Than Thirty Families

Four People Injured Jumping from Windows to Escape

Xu Zhang, a resident of No. 17 Beiwang Yima Alley inside Xinbeimen, rented a room to Xu Daqian (54 years old) from Changzhou. Yesterday morning at 7:30 AM, Xu was careless with fire, and within moments, clouds of smoke filled the air and broke through the roof. The nearby patrol police learned of the fire and immediately notified the fire brigades of each district, which quickly rushed to the scene with pump trucks to extinguish the fire. It took about two hours to extinguish the fire. In addition to the complete destruction of the house and belongings of No. 17, the fire also spread to the houses at No. 19 and No. 21, affecting a total of more than ten houses and thirty families, causing considerable damage. At that time, Chen Xiaohu from Suzhou and others, who lived on the upper floor of No. 17, were unable to escape and jumped out of the windows in desperation. Chen injured his mouth, his wife Yu injured her head and feet, and their daughter Er'nan injured her feet. In addition, Chen's apprentice, Cheng San, injured both his hands and feet. Shen Zhenhua, the chief of the Second Precinct of the First District of the Municipal Public Safety Bureau, led the police to suppress the fire and sent the injured to Shanghai Hospital for treatment.

Thefts Also Reported

Hongkou 217

Yu Fengyong Southern Goods Store, No. 1036 North Szechuan Road in Hongkou, managed by Zhang Muxian, has been in business for many years and is doing quite well, which has made it a target for thieves. At 5:30 PM the day before yesterday, three thieves, speaking with a local accent and wearing short cloth shirts and pants, suddenly appeared. One thief guarded the door, while the other two, armed with guns, broke into the store, first threatening all the employees and monitoring their actions. Then, one of the thieves proceeded to loot cash worth 111 yuan, 72 jiao in small silver coins, and 14 jiao in fractional notes. After the thieves fled with the stolen goods, an apprentice at the store reported the robbery and the amount of the loss to the patrol police at No. 26 of the Fifth Precinct of the Municipal Public Safety Bureau, who reported it to District Chief Jin Gong. The District Chief quickly dispatched a patrol inspector and a police sergeant with police officers to the scene to search for the thieves, but the thieves had already vanished without a trace.

Nanshi 218

At 1:45 PM yesterday, three thieves suddenly entered the home of Xu Bohua at No. 9 Ankang Lane, Da Wang Miao Street in Nanshi. All three were wearing black clothes and spoke with a Jiangbei accent. After entering the door, they showed their guns and forced Xu's family members into a corner, ordering them to remain silent. Then, they divided into groups and searched the rooms, overturning chests and boxes, and looting cash, silver, gold jewelry, and other items worth several tens of yuan. They left with the stolen goods and scattered in all directions.

West Shanghai 219

At about 1:15 AM yesterday, three thieves came to the home of Huang Kengting, from Yancheng, who rents out rickshaws for a living, at No. 2 Tiejiang Lane, Route Ghisi, Caojiadu, West Shanghai. Pretending to pay rickshaw rent, they knocked on the door and shouted loudly. Huang's wife believed them and woke up from her dream to open the door. The three thieves, one with a pistol and one with a sharp knife, rushed in and ordered her to remain silent. They immediately turned over chests and boxes, looting a gold bracelet, a gold ring, a pair of gold earrings, and 100 small silver coins, for a total loss of more than 300 yuan. As the thieves were escaping with the stolen goods, the victim discovered that the pistol held by one of the thieves was fake. He then boldly gave chase, shouting for the capture of the thieves. At that time, the neighbors heard the alarm and rushed out to help capture them, but the thieves had already fled far away without a trace. The victim then wrote a report and submitted it to the nearby Sixth District Police Station, requesting the pursuit, arrest, and investigation of the thieves and stolen goods.

The Public Works Bureau Will Establish Three Additional Construction Permit Offices After Moving to the City Center 220

The Public Works Bureau is scheduled to move to the city center on the 25th. To facilitate the issuance of permits for construction-related matters such as reconstruction, construction, and demolition within the city, three additional offices will be established to handle the issuance of permits within the city. Details are as follows: (1) The City Center Permit Office will handle the application and issuance of permits for all types of projects in all districts of the city. (2) Effective immediately, the South Shanghai District Permit Office will be established at No. 952 Zhonghua Road, within the South Shanghai District Road Engineering Management Office. In addition to handling the application and issuance of permits within the district, it will also handle the application and issuance of permits for the Caojing District. (3) Effective January 1, 1934, the West Shanghai District Permit Office will be established at the first house of the new village at the intersection of Yu Garden Road and Route Bay, east of Zhaofeng Park, to handle the application and issuance of permits for the Fahua and Puji districts. (4) The permit offices in the Zhabei, Wusong, Yangjing, and Gaoqiao districts will remain at their original locations, and their operations will remain unchanged. (5) The permit offices in the Jiangwan and Yinxiang districts, as well as the West Shanghai Office, will be closed at the end of this month. (6) The districts of Gaohang, Luhang, Tangqiao, Yangsi, Yinhang, Pengpu, Zhenru, and Caojing will continue to be handled by the Municipal Commissioners' Offices as before.

Water Disconnection Just Resolved

Landlords Demand Extra Fees

Water Disaster Relief Association Letter Soliciting Donations 223

Victims Exposed to the Elements, in Dire Need of Assistance

Donations Remitted, Solicitation Continues

The Shanghai Charity Organizations' Joint Association for Soliciting Donations for the Yellow River Water Disaster Relief, recognizing that the weather is becoming increasingly cold and that the victims are suffering from both hunger and cold and are in dire need of assistance, has specifically sent letters to all fundraisers, requesting them to remit the donations they have already collected as soon as possible for relief efforts. The original text reads: "Esteemed Sirs, in the past, due to the Yellow River bursting its banks, the provinces of Hebei, Shandong, Henan, and Shaanxi have all suffered severe flooding, with cities and villages submerged, the dead washed away, and the living wailing in despair. The pitiful situation is difficult to describe in words, and the matter of providing relief is of utmost urgency. However, the disaster is deep and the affected area is vast, relying on the collective efforts of all. We have previously sent donation registers, earnestly requesting generous donations. We trust that you have taken notice. We have now received numerous letters and telegrams from the special commissioners in various relief areas, reporting that houses in the disaster areas have either been buried under sand and soil or are still submerged in water. The victims are exposed to the elements, enduring wind and meals [without proper shelter], crying from hunger and cold. Those who have not died from the floods are on the verge of death from cold and starvation. They urgently hope for a rapid collection of substantial funds to be allocated for relief. We have long admired your compassion and empathy. Saving the distressed and rescuing the drowning have always been your shared sentiment. Therefore, we do not hesitate to bother you and write again, respectfully requesting that you promptly remit the donations you have already collected. For those who have not yet solicited, please continue to do so and provide a steady stream of assistance to save those sorrowful geese. We are most eagerly awaiting your response."

Son-in-Law Refuses to Provide Living Expenses, Mother-in-Law Forcibly Takes Daughter Away 224

A woman from Gaoyou, Xie Wan's daughter, Xiao Gui Zi, residing at 957 Dong You Heng Road, is 23 years old and possesses some beauty. She has been living with You Da Jin, a fellow villager residing at No. 10 Kunshan Garden, Kunshan Road, for four years and has a daughter named Xiao Hong Zi, who is only two years old and whom she cherishes dearly. Xie Wan's monthly living expenses were provided by You. Recently, due to You's income being insufficient to cover expenses, this payment has been discontinued. Xie has repeatedly negotiated, but payment has been delayed. Xie became greatly angered and, at around 3 PM on the afternoon of the previous day, gathered several people and went to You's house to reason with him. You happened to be out. Xie then forcibly took her daughter, Xiao Gui Zi, and her granddaughter, Xiao Hong Zi, and fled, disappearing without a trace. Upon You's return, after learning of the situation, he went to Xie's house on Dong You Heng Road to make a scene, demanding the return of Xiao Gui Zi and her daughter. Xie also spoke rudely, and they quarreled with each other. Neighbors gathered in large numbers. An investigator from the Huishan Patrol Station passed by, inquired about the situation, and took Xie Wan to the patrol station. Yesterday morning, she was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The patrol station's lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, explained the situation and requested an extension for further investigation. Subsequently, Xie Xiao Gui Zi claimed that the defendant was her mother. At the time, her mother brought several people to the house, and her daughter Hong Zi was taken away by an unknown person, Mr. Jia. She herself was dragged to the South Railway Station and took the opportunity to slip away. She does not know where Xiao Hong Zi is now. When questioned, Xie Wan claimed that Xiao Hong Zi was actually taken away and hidden by the Wan family, the family of Xiao Gui Zi's former fiancé, and had nothing to do with her. She asked for consideration. Judge Wu Zehan ordered that the woman be temporarily detained in her current location and rescheduled the hearing to clarify the facts.

City Government Approves Dredging of Silt from Wharf for Ships 225

Xing Zhigang, representative of the shipping companies of Pudong West, requested the dredging of the shoals along the Pu River south of Wharf No. 16 to maintain navigation and revitalize commerce. The Shanghai Municipal Government has approved it, stating: "Received the submission. After instructing the Bureau of Public Works and the Bureau of Public Utilities to jointly submit a report, it was found that the dredging of the shoals along the Pu River has always been planned by the Dredging Bureau. After the Bureau of Public Works inquired with the Dredging Bureau, it received a reply that the shoal section had been dredged between 1931 and 1932 and would not need to be dredged again until around 1935. The current proposal for dredging cannot be approved. However, it was stated that if one or two wharves in that section need to be repaired, a clamshell dredger could be dispatched to work for about a week. Based on the previous order, we jointly submitted a report for your review." According to this, in addition to the instruction, it is appropriate to approve and inform. It is heard that the representative is requesting the Bureau of Public Works to dredge the shallowest areas of the Nanhui Guan and the Gongyi Shipping Company wharves to facilitate navigation.

The Precursor to the Northwest Trading Company 226

The Northwest Trading Company was initiated by a current director of a Gansu province department, and since its preparation was undertaken by former Senator Zhao Shiyu, he has spared no effort. Prominent figures in Shanghai, such as Wang Rutang, Xue Dubi, Chen Zhishuo, and Zhang Xinwu, are said to have been invited to join as promoters, demonstrating the Chinese people's determination to develop the Northwest. Recently, various authorities in the Northwest, in order to facilitate the company's progress, telegraphed Zhao and others to go to Long to personally discuss plans. To clarify the content of the company to all sectors, the origin is now revealed as follows: "Establishing a nation globally, national systems differ, policies vary with time, but the ultimate goal is national prosperity and benefit for the people. This is universally acknowledged by those who discuss politics and national theory. National prosperity is based on the people's benefit. In ancient times, it was called 'promoting well-being and utilizing resources'; today, it is called 'social economy,' both focusing on the people's livelihood as the top priority. The principle of people's livelihood varies with the degree of a nation's economic progress. At a minimum, it must ensure adequate food and clothing, preventing hunger and cold, so that social order can be maintained and national turmoil can be avoided. There is a way to ensure the people's livelihood: benefiting from the natural resources also depends on human effort. Trading cloth for silk, exchanging grain for machinery, was the case in ancient times. With the world open and the market expanded, the economic state has also progressed from simple to complex. Chinese economy has suffered direct and indirect exploitation by imperialists. Raw materials are sold cheaply, finished goods are bought at high prices, leading to rural bankruptcy and increasing people's hardship. The Southeast, with convenient transportation, has gradually reformed this problem. The Northwest, located in remote areas, often has its raw materials remain unutilized, such as wool, leather, cotton, and other important industrial raw materials. Due to the lack of transportation and sales organizations, foreign merchants and compradores manipulate and buy them at low prices, while daily necessities require high prices. Thus, on one hand, some are rich and corrupt, while on the other hand, some cry from hunger and cold. Production and sales are out of sync, and supply and demand are not met. This is a concern for society and people's livelihood, and it is what those who advocate developing the Northwest should urgently plan for. Recognizing this, we have initiated a Northwest Trading Company to adjust production and sales, meeting supply and demand, so that the raw materials produced in the Northwest provinces can be transported and sold to areas where manufacturing industries need them at fair prices. In return, it will transport and sell goods for daily use to the Northwest provinces at fair prices, to prevent the monopoly of foreign merchants and compradores, to meet the urgent needs of the people's daily life. Farmers, industrialists, and merchants will all benefit, and tax revenue agencies will also increase legitimate income, reducing excessive levies, alleviating people's hardship. However, creation is difficult and relies on the strength of the group. We respectfully present a general overview and hope that all national elites, those who are committed to developing the Northwest and alleviating the people's livelihood, will step forward to guide us. We would be most grateful."

Citizens' 32nd District Association Requests Streetlight Installation 230

The members of the 32nd District Branch of the Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Association, Erwo Leather Goods Company, noting that the lights in the Gansu Road area are few and far between and the gas lamps are dim, making it easy for petty criminals to hide and posing a danger to pedestrians, sent a letter to the association requesting them to forward a letter to the Public Works Bureau to install additional streetlights in the Gansu Road area to prevent danger. Biscuit Guild Discusses Unwarranted Fine Case 231

Requests All Organizations to Unanimously Assist in Negotiations

The Shanghai Biscuit and Confectionery Guild convened its 23rd joint meeting of executive and supervisory committee members yesterday. Zhang Yichen was elected chairman. A member of the Dehua Biscuit Company reported that a receipt for 88 cents had a one-cent stamp affixed to it, but the Committee for the Trial of Cases Violating the Stamp Tax Regulations fined them five yuan, which was enforced by the Second District Public Security Bureau, without allowing any opportunity for defense. The guild's representative sent a letter requesting withdrawal, but was told that the fine had already been enforced and paid and transferred to the Public Security Bureau, so the request could not be processed. After discussion, it was unanimously felt that the Committee's trial of cases was hasty, based on emotions, and abused the power to fine. The inspectors sought to gain merit and reward, and the superiors and subordinates conspired to harm the merchants. If the merchants remain silent in pain, the consequences will be dire. The guild, having purported to try cases violating the Stamp Tax Regulations, cannot dismiss the matter with a few words because the fine was small, had already been enforced, and could not be processed. For example, someone charged with a crime is allowed to appeal and request a retrial. It has never been heard of that a case, once discussed in a chamber, becomes an ironclad case. Therefore, it is imperative to request that the fine be refunded. In another case, the Committee deemed the account notification of the Taichang Company to be a disguised invoice, falsely accusing them of taking advantage of loopholes, and fined them 20 yuan. In fact, according to commercial practice, it was a simple notification with no relation to payments. However, the Stamp Committee considered it to have the nature of monetary receipts and payments, deemed the failure to affix a stamp a violation, and punished them accordingly. According to the facts, if this is punishable, then bank and money shop statements, and lawyers' warnings for overdue payments, have the same meaning and function, and have never been heard of being punished. Why be lenient to them and harsh to us? In summary, there are countless cases of being fined for not deserving punishment due to stamp duty issues. It was unanimously believed that this kind of event is a common problem for the entire business community, not just the Dehua and Taichang companies suffering. All merchants should express their opinion. It is proposed to send a letter to all industry guilds and district citizens' associations in the city, submitting the matter for discussion, jointly seeking a solution to alleviate the pain, and unanimously supporting the companies.

Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau Publicly Claims Drugs and Organizational Items 233

Will Be Disposed of According to Law If Not Claimed by Deadline

The Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau Chief, Wen Hongen, sent a letter to this newspaper stating: "According to the report from the Third Branch of the Fifth District, 'On November 19th, it was reported that a number of Japanese and Korean people were seen entering and exiting No. 14 Qingyangli, Yangjiahang Road, acting suspiciously. Patrol Officer Wang Youheng was dispatched to handle the matter. Subsequently, it was reported that he, along with Police Inspector Yamashiro and Officer Ozawa from the Japanese Consular Police Station, went to the residence on the same day. A young man came out to meet them, stating, "I live in the attic. The owner is currently not here and will return around 6 PM. My name is Li Shuishan, and I am 21 years old." At 6:30 PM, they went to the residence again with personnel from the Japanese Consulate and discovered various drugs and equipment for manufacturing heroin on the third floor. The items in the room were all Japanese daily necessities. No one was found in the residence. A report was submitted for review.' We immediately ordered them to verify the furniture and other items with personnel from the Japanese Consulate, compile a list, and have Yamashiro Zenpei from the Japanese Consular Police Station come to verify the list in detail the next day. Both parties signed and sealed the list, each keeping a copy as proof. The identity of the residence's tenant, Lin Rongchang, whether Japanese or Korean, could not be determined. However, Li Shuishan, whom they glimpsed on the 19th, was confirmed to be Korean. Lin Rongchang had secretly moved into No. 14 Qingyangli in October of this year without reporting to the Household Registration Office of this station, secretly setting up a drug manufacturing facility in the house. An investigation was conducted for several days before it was cracked. Lin Rongchang and Li Shuishan have both reportedly fled. We are submitting the heroin manufacturing equipment, drugs, furniture, and other items, along with the list, for your review and instructions.' Furniture, drugs, a motor, a list, and other items have been submitted to the bureau. We have written to the Japanese Consulate General for verification, but it is still unclear whether the drug manufacturing facility was established by Japanese residents. In view of this, after investigating the items seized in this case, the owner's name and address are repeatedly unconfirmed. In addition to various drugs and equipment used for committing crimes, there are also various furniture and clothing items. It is urgent to issue a public notice to claim them, in order to show fairness. In addition to issuing a public notice and sending a letter to the Japanese Consulate General to forward the notice to the owner, we are setting a deadline of six months from December 20th of this year for them to come to the bureau to identify and claim the items. If no one claims the items by the deadline, the bureau will dispose of the aforementioned furniture and other evidence in accordance with the law. We hereby inform you to investigate and refer to this notice and hope that you will publish it in the news section so that the owner can be informed and come to the bureau to claim the items by the deadline." Sincerely, Shanghai Newspaper Office.

The book is divided into seven lessons, totaling sixty-four pages, six and a half inches long, and four and a half inches wide, with a three-color cover. The teaching materials are novel, clear, and easy to understand. It can be learned in seven days and completed in one month. With focused practice, one can record eighty to ninety words per minute. Those who are illiterate can learn to read and write after learning shorthand, and those who are already literate can write faster. It is truly a great contribution to Chinese culture. For the sake of popularization, Mr. Yang is selling each book for only forty cents. An 80% discount is offered for pre-orders. The book is scheduled to be released on January 15th of the Gregorian calendar. Weather Report 244

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather is quite cold, with gentle northwest to north winds around Shandong. There is fog in the Yangtze River basin and this area in the morning. The wind is gentle, coming from the southwest to northwest. Along the coast south of Ma'an Island, the sky is cloudy and the northeast wind is quite tight. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 52.9 degrees, and the lowest was 27.7 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 57.9 degrees, and the lowest was 42.8 degrees.

The Xujiahui Observatory also issued a weather forecast for the Shanghai and Hangzhou areas during the Christmas period yesterday, saying that the weather will be clear and not very cold, with fog in the morning and gentle west winds. However, after Tuesday and Wednesday, the weather will be colder and cloudier, with tightening northwest to northeast winds.

Letter 245

To the Editor: Having read the article "Resolution of the Water Outage Case in Tonghai Lane" in your newspaper yesterday, I found that the description of the process was quite erroneous. After the water outage incident in this lane occurred, all the tenants jointly elected Liu Zhenbo, Tang Fengming, Chen Shirong, and Chen Wenyun to petition the Public Works Department for assistance. At that time, the owner did not go along with them. Until 2:00 PM, the Public Works Department had not yet come to open the Taiping faucet. The residents, having been without water for many days, were in imminent danger. They had no choice but to automatically open the Taiping faucet in the lane to alleviate the emergency. At that time, the owner sent a representative, Mr. Yao, to participate in the water outage meeting and agreed to write to the water company to send someone to open the water pipes for the residents. The facts of the matter are as described above. The news published yesterday was issued by the Xinsheng News Agency, but the agency did not come to investigate, resulting in a misrepresentation. I hope you will make a correction. Sincerely, Representatives of the Tenants of Tonghai Lane, Liu Zhenbo, Tang Fengming, Chen Shirong, Chen Wenyun.

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Learning 246

— Jianfen

Friends: When you "study" at school, do you feel that "singing"! (or the subjects you understand)! is very interesting, while "arithmetic"! (or the subjects you don't understand)! is tasteless? The reason is very obvious, it's because of "understanding" and "not understanding." Because the rhythm of "singing" is clear, it feels interesting to sing; the truth of "arithmetic" is not understood, so it's tasteless to do. If this is indeed the case for you, then I now have a way to make "arithmetic"! (or the subjects you don't understand)! as interesting as "singing"! (or the subjects you understand)! That is, when the teacher is lecturing, when dissecting the truth, you have to "listen carefully." If there is anything you don't understand, you can raise it and "ask" until you "understand." Don't abandon it just because it's tasteless. You must know that the Englishman Watt himself studied the use of "steam" and invented the "steam engine"; how can we, now having teachers guiding us in "lessons," fail to understand the truth and find it tasteless?

Spartan Children's Training 247

— Shouwu

Sparta was a country with a martial spirit. The people were very strong. Because there was a wise royal family member named Li Kouergusi, he made many rules to train the people.

When a baby was first born, his father had to wrap him in a robe and send him to the council, where many old and wise people would examine him. If he was strong and had no physical disabilities, he would be returned to the father to be raised; otherwise, he would be abandoned in the mountains.

When children reached the age of seven, they left their parents and were taken care of by people selected by the state. The books they read were all stories of heroes and wars. All year round, from morning to night, they were only allowed to wear a single garment of coarse wool. They slept without a bed, on a pile of reeds. In winter, they were only allowed to add a layer of cattail fluff.

Do Your Best 248

— Wang Zhong

There was a farmer who was cultivating a large field. The rice was about to dry up because there was no rain. The farmer was very worried, looking at the sky every day, wondering if it would rain.

At this time, a little rain in the sky saw him and said, "Ah! Poor farmer, you have used so much effort, and the rice is about to dry up. I want to help you with a little rain." Another little rain said, "How can you, with your little rain, nourish such a large field?" The first little rain said, "Yes, but when I go down, at least I can comfort him." The second little rain saw the first little rain falling and landing right on the farmer's head. He also immediately went down, saying, "Let me also nourish his rice."

At this time, a large group of rain came running and said, "You are doing such a good thing, we want to do it too."

After a rain, the rice in the field ripened. It was all because of a little bit of rain wanting to do its best.

Precious Sister 249

— Mai Ying

The sun had set, and Precious Sister stood at the door of her house, waiting for her older sister to return from work. Several large trees across the street were to be cut down, as they obscured the road in front, preventing her from seeing her older sister sooner.

Her older sister emerged from the woods, and Precious Sister ran up to her. Calling out "Older Sister," she took the older sister's lunch basket into her own hands. She opened the basket lid to see if there was any leftover rice and vegetables.

She told her older sister: Mother's illness has not improved, and Father has gone to Mr. Xu's house to borrow rice. Her older sister said nothing, just sighed.

Her older sister's face was much thinner. She said to her sister: Older sister, I am stronger now, and I can carry half a bucket of river water and run back. Tomorrow, you can rest at home, and I will go to work in your place. Her older sister said nothing, just smiled bitterly.

Children! Guess why those four children are clapping and laughing as he climbs the tree? 250

New Stories 251

— Yin Feng

▲Naughty Children and Frogs

A group of naughty children were playing by a small pond. Suddenly, they saw several frogs in the pond. They picked up small stones by the pond. When the frogs' heads came out of the water, they all threw stones at them, clapping and laughing when they hit.

"Children," said a frog, "this is not a game. Although you are looking for fun, we are in mortal danger."

▲Mother Crab and Baby Crab

The mother crab said to the baby crab: "Child, why do you always walk crookedly like this? You must walk straight!"

"Mother," said the baby crab, "please walk and show me so I can learn how to walk like you."

But the mother crab tried several times, but could never walk straight, so the baby crab just laughed at the mother crab's lesson.

Human Body Conversation 252

— Wu Yuan

▲Don't Sigh

The brain said to the two hands: "Please, you two, help me. I'm in great difficulty!"

The hands said: "Helping is possible, but we want you to agree to a condition!"

"What condition?"

"Please tell the mouth not to sigh anymore!"

The brain said: "What's the reason for that?"

The two hands said: "Because we are most afraid of sighing; when the mouth sighs, we can't do anything! In the future, as long as you tell the mouth to clench its teeth and hold its breath, then no matter how difficult things are, we ten brothers (fingers) will have a way to deal with them!"

▲Cooperation

The mouth said to the hand: "You and I should really cooperate!"

"What's the reason?" the hand said.

The mouth said: "Because I can connect with you in everything. For example: you can kill people, and I can eat people; you can hit people, and I can scold people!"

The hand said, "But I can support people!"

The mouth said, "I...I can say good things?"

"Saying good things has nothing to do with supporting people!" the hand said. "I am still supporting people when you say good things; I am still supporting people when you don't say good things!"

▲The Greatest

The ear and the eye chatted, discussing the "greatest" thing.

The ear said, "According to what I have heard: the sound of machines 'clicking' is the greatest; everything in human society is progressing along with this sound!"

The eye said, "According to what I have seen: the ten numbers 1234567890 are the greatest; the fate of human society is governed by these ten numbers!"

The mouth, hearing this from the side, asked the ear and the eye, "Please judge: what should I say to be considered the greatest?"

"According to us: it is the greatest when you don't open your mouth; because no matter what it is, once you say it, the great becomes small!" the ear and the eye replied in unison.

Guess the Candy 253

— Xu Zongjie

"Come and see! Guess and play!" The hawker sang loudly, attracting children. What's in the pan? Preserved tangerine peel and caramel. What's in hand? Hundreds of guessing paper slips. One copper coin for a guess, tears welling up when you guess wrong.

Here, the civet cat replaces the crown prince; there, the restoration goes to Nanyang; there are also colors divided into red, yellow, blue, white, and black; there is also one, two, three, and four to ponder. There are many patterns, and once greed arises, you are fooled.

Children! Don't taste it lightly. If you get used to gambling from a young age, it will be difficult to correct when you grow up. We want to eat candy and fruit, so we buy good quality goods from the store. It is best to save this spare money and donate it to aviation to strengthen national defense.

The Ending of Deception 254

— Nai Chang

Yesha was a strong child with blood-red hair; but he didn't want to do anything all day long, just thinking about playing and deceiving people. One afternoon, he pretended to be a cripple and begged for food.

"Pity a poor donkey with a crippled leg! Give me a few copper coins!"

Just then, a child named Heli passed by him. Seeing his miserable fate, he gave him some money.

Many days later, in another place, Yesha pretended to be blind. Heli passed by here again. Seeing that this was the same one who had a crippled leg before, he immediately understood. He pretended to be compassionate and promised to take Yesha home to treat him well. When they arrived home, Heli led him into the large wooden pen, closed the door, and then said to Yesha:

"Friend, open your eyes and see what place this is! Why do you want to deceive people?"

After being imprisoned, Yesha never dared to deceive people again.

One Copper Coin 255

— Shi Yusheng

As usual, Mom gave me ten copper coins for breakfast money. But today, I hesitated when I reached the door of the steamed bun shop.

Didn't the teacher say? Under such circumstances, Chinese children should be diligent and self-reliant, and should not seek oral pleasure! Don't you see those little compatriots in the Northeast? Poor things! They are Chinese, but they can't even read Chinese books! They can no longer read the motherland's language with their parents, and must learn that Japanese language! Can I seek oral pleasure and not rescue my little compatriots? 丨丨 No, I must save at least one copper coin every day as a savings for aviation to save the country!

"Three copper coins each"! The sharp shout of the pancake seller. I unhesitatingly took out nine copper coins.

The old clerk of the steamed bun shop looked at me strangely; but he didn't know the taste of me chewing dry pancakes!

A Grain of Wheat 256

— Jin Xi

There was a grain of wheat, hiding in the barn and sighing.

It guessed that in a few days, the terrible farmer would bury them alive in the lower layer of the soil. It did not want such a cruel encounter, so it worried and sighed.

The terrible day finally arrived, but this grain of wheat was very clever, and actually escaped the farmer's attention. It could still hide safely in the barn.

It was happy, but also sad. Sad because all of its companions left the barn, and for a long time, there was no friend to talk to it.

The following spring, a large batch of new wheat entered the barn. Those were the sons of last year's companions.

So this grain of wheat regretted it. It said: "A grain of wheat that is not buried in the mud is still a grain and will rot; if it is not afraid of being buried, it will produce many grains."

Where did the younger brother come from? 257

— Xue Fan

"Daddy earns silver ingots, Mom adds a younger brother..." Huimin sat alone on the doorstep singing; but in a flash, he suddenly thought that Mom added a younger brother, where did the younger brother come from? He hurried to his mother.

"Mom! You're going to give me another younger brother, where does this younger brother come from?"

"Child"! The mother said, laughing: "You'll understand this when you grow up; you see, the cat in our house is about to have kittens, you wait and see."

Huimin, hearing this answer, was just suspicious. Every day he went to the cat's nest to look at the cat. The cat couldn't explain anything, just meowed at Huimin.

Willing Children 258

— Aiqing

It was very cold today, but school still required gymnastics, because Teacher Liu had said: "To have a good physique and spirit, you must train in this cold weather." Wang Sida, a third-grade student, valued this sentence very much, so his body was very strong.

One morning, Wang Sida saw the gymnastics teacher practicing boxing alone on the playground. He suddenly thought: "No wonder the principal likes and praises the gymnastics teacher so much. This is because he works hard himself, and that's why the result is so good!"

A child who is willing to work hard will definitely have good fortune in the future.

Animal Tails 259

— Bingyu

▲ Tails Used as Replacement for Feet

The kangaroo's tail is large and powerful. When its two hind legs stand upright, the tail must lean against the ground to support its body. Sometimes, it uses its tail to support its entire body and then kicks at its enemy with its hind legs.

▲ Tails Used for Cold Protection

The squirrel's tail, when it runs back and forth on branches, can both balance its body's inclination and protect its body's temperature.

▲ Tails that Signal Danger

When a deer in the mountains encounters a different kind of ferocious beast, its tail immediately stands up, and the white fur below the tail becomes even more prominent. Whenever it encounters an enemy, this white fur part shakes especially, conveying the meaning of "The enemy is coming, be careful!" to its fellows.

▲ Tails Usable as Rudders

The sea beaver in the ocean is good at swimming, and its tail is different from other animals. The shape of the tail is flat and without fur. When swimming, it is like a rudder for steering a boat.

Correspondence from a Young Friend in the Countryside 260

— Ziming

▲ Introduction

My little friends:

Many little friends, although newly acquainted, have been spiritually connected for a long time. However, through recent correspondence, it seems we have become even closer. It seems a further understanding of me is also needed. I must say a few words:

In my previous letter, I called myself "Xiang Lao" [Country Elder]. You little friends must be wondering: "Is he an old man from the countryside?" "Is he a rustic old man?" ... pondering over the word "old." Friends, my little friends, my appellation "Xiang Lao" has absolutely no such meaning. Initially, I used these two words because I have long lived in the countryside and have been accompanied by this great nature year-round. Indeed, I have a great affection for the countryside. I miss it, and it cherishes me, so much so that I cannot separate from it. Because, in my time and your time, we were held in its embrace, jumping and dancing. And now, in your time, you meet your little friends at its knees. Singing happy songs every day, everyone is happy and harmonious, searching for the bright road to the future. A march is playing right now!

Little friends, do you know me now? Do you understand the meaning of "Xiang Lao"? Please use your intelligent brains to understand!

Goodbye!

▲ Lingering Autumn

Little friends:

How strange! The autumn wind, like a chaste woman, has actually put on a fierce face these past few days, "roaring and howling." I wonder who angered it? Compared to when it was kind and lovely, driving away the "sweltering heat" of the world and bringing a gentle "autumn" for humanity, it is truly "like two different people."

Oh! The aged skin color has the air of "approaching death." Knowing that the end is near, it gives a final, mad cry: Perhaps it fears that a poisonous world is about to descend and cannot bear for humanity to be trampled upon! However, "hoarse and exhausted," it finally overcomes the fierce god with "bared fangs and claws" and a "ferocious face!"

Many, many trees have all changed their clothes, wearing mourning clothes, the earth is all white, quietly indicating that this chaste woman has "died peacefully in her bed."

Little friends! Is a chilling atmosphere enveloping us? So many precious youth of us humans are being stripped away like this. Catch up quickly! Don't lament! Don't waste time!

Goodbye!

(1)

Min'er said to Ya Wan: "When you lock your room door and go out, why don't you tell the people at home? I had to search everywhere for you!" Ya Wan said, "I wrote it on a piece of paper and put it on the table in my room. Didn't you see it?"

(2)

The mother came back from outside, and the son couldn't see clearly who it was, so he asked loudly, "What are you here for?" The mother said angrily, "Do you know me?" The son said, "Oh! It's Mother. Then, don't you know I'm nearsighted?"

(3)

I always have to turn off the lights when I sleep at night. Last night, at twelve o'clock, Song'er woke up, couldn't see anything in the darkness, and started crying. We were woken up by him and quickly asked him why he was crying. He said, "Daddy! My eyes are blind!"

(4)

Ya Zhen bought a goose. He happened to need to relieve himself, so he had to put the goose on the ground and run into the public toilet. Unexpectedly, someone replaced it with a duck. When Ya Zhen came out and looked at it, he said, "How strange! I only left for a moment, and it's already become so thin and small?"

Education News: Other Locations

Beijing City's Education Expenses Prepared for Independence 264

▲ Planning to Establish a Senior Vocational School

Because the Ministry of Education hopes that the educational expenses of all provinces and cities will be independent, the Nanjing Municipal Government, together with the Ministry of Education's supervisors, discussed the measures for the independence of Beijing City's education expenses a few days ago. It is reported that the principle of educational expense independence has been agreed upon. The municipal government has ordered the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to draft detailed plans, which generally involve designating several items such as housing donations, central subsidies, and other funds from the municipal government, and organizing a management committee to be responsible for supervision. The educational expenses will be stored separately to ensure thorough independence.

It is also heard that in the near future, the municipal government plans to reorganize and expand the junior vocational schools and establish senior vocational schools. Because the estimated start-up cost is about 400,000 yuan, it plans to request subsidies from the Boxer Indemnity Committee on the one hand and raise funds independently by the municipal government on the other hand. This kind of senior vocational school is also being planned, but it will take a little longer than the expansion of the junior vocational schools.

Opinions of Ministry of Education Commissioner Li Ximou on Education in Anhui and Jiangxi 265

▲ Ordinary Subject Teaching Methods Lack Experimentation

▲ Vocational Education Equipment and Teachers are Quite Lacking

Ministry of Education Commissioner Li Ximou, after inspecting education in Anhui and Jiangxi provinces, is currently compiling a detailed report on the inspection of the two provinces. Here is a record of the situation of the two provinces' finances and points that should be generally noted, based on personal conversations.

▲ Financial Situation of Education (1) The educational expenses of Anhui Province are more than 2.6 million yuan annually, of which 1.2 million yuan is the central subsidy, and the remaining more than 1.4 million yuan is provided by the provincial treasury. The central subsidy is received monthly, and the provincial expenses are relatively short. The province's educational expenses are independent, and there is the establishment of an Educational Expenses Management Office, responsible for the collection and expenditure of funds. (2) The educational expenses of Jiangxi Province are 2 million yuan annually, which is the salt surtax. The funds are allocated by the Western Shore Salt Transport Bureau established by the Ministry of Finance. The province's educational expenses are independent and there is a management committee to supervise the use of the funds, and a management office is responsible for the collection and expenditure of expenses. However, the educational expense independence of the above two provinces is not as good as the direct collection of educational expenses by the Jiangsu Educational Expenses Management Office.

Points that should be noted: It is heard that the following are common points that should be noted in both provinces: (1) For the teaching methods of ordinary subjects, teachers only use textbooks for teaching. Classrooms lack scientific instruments for experimentation, so that subjects such as physics and chemistry lack objects to prove and experiment with, reducing students' interest. (2) For social education (popular education, adult education), there is a lack of corresponding organizers and leaders. This situation is mostly due to the lack of adequate preparation for training talents before the event. (3) Vocational education is extremely lacking in equipment and teachers, and too little emphasis is placed on local handicrafts, resulting in poor products that cannot compete with foreign goods. It is hoped that teachers in primary and secondary schools in various places will have refresher opportunities during the summer vacation to supplement their knowledge and skills.

(10)(5) The Wuxi Normal School proposed how to make the educational subjects of normal schools themselves labor-oriented. Resolved: (1) When normal schools enroll new students, the Education Bureau must notify them in advance according to their needs to determine the reference for the quota.

(3) Normal schools should report the students of the county to the Education Bureau every semester for review. Shanghai Branch of the China Scientific Movement Association Established Yesterday 269

▲ Report on Preparations and Discussion of the Constitution

▲ The First Year's Work Outline Was Also Decided

The Shanghai Branch of the China Scientific Movement Association has been in preparation for several months. The inaugural meeting was held at 3 p.m. yesterday at the Shanghai Lianhuan Club on Sanma Road. The preparation process was reported, and the draft constitution was discussed. The opening meeting is recorded as follows:

Attending Members 270

Including Chen Jinmin, Tong Xingbai, Xu Zeye, Lin Meiyan, Wu Yun'chu, Yan Zhenyu, Huang Ya'e, Wu Gengzhi, Hu Lizhen, Jiang Gongchen, Yang Sili, Wang Zushun, Wang Keming, Zhang Gao, Gong Benshan, Ping Zuyuan, Zhou Zanming, Zhao Qiyuan, Chen Zhenhua, Wang Dexun, Wang Mo, Guo Zongda, Dai Yuheng, Zhang Huaisheng, Huang Yongping, Wei Yunping, Wu Zhuo, Hu Ningsheng, Hu Zhaosheng, Xu Chunting, Shao Jialin, and more than fifty others.

Chairman's Report 271

Chairman Chen Jinmin, recorder Xu Zeye, first the chairman reported on the preparation process, saying that during the summer vacation, in a corner of Shanghai, there was already a brewing of organizing a national body to carry out the scientific movement. Two major policies were drafted: (1) Establish a scientific experiment hall to provide science experiments for primary and secondary schools in this city, so as to change the scientific education and become the center of the scientific movement. (2) Organize groups to be the driving force for the implementation of the scientific movement. At that time, I submitted an outline to Mr. Pan Gongzhan and Tao Baichuan to forward it to Mayor Wu, trying to find ways to help. Mayor Wu immediately agreed to allocate a portion of the Fenglin Bridge site, after the municipal government moved to the central district, as the site of the scientific experiment hall, which is currently in progress. By chance, Mr. Zhang Beihai, the secretary of the Nanjing General Assembly, came to Shanghai to prepare for the Shanghai Branch of the Scientific Movement, and recommended me as the director of the preparation. After several meetings, it was established today. Then, the constitution was revised.

Work Outline 272

Graduates of Schools That Have Not Reported School Status Will Not Be Allowed to Take the Joint Graduation Exam 275

Those Who Have Reported but Whose Supporting Documents Have Not Been Verified

Are Allowed to Participate First, and Certificates Will Be Issued After Verification

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order yesterday to municipal and registered private secondary schools in this city, stating that the joint secondary school graduation examination for this academic year will be held soon. Whether or not the graduating students of each school should be allowed to participate in this joint examination is based on the school status of new and transfer students reported by each school in each academic year. If schools fail to report student school status on schedule as ordered, resulting in the Education Bureau having no basis for verification, the graduating students will not be allowed to participate in the joint examination or graduation examination. For those who have already reported the school status of new and transfer students, but whose supporting documents have not been verified, and the student's school status has not been verified, a flexible approach may be adopted, allowing them to participate in the joint examination and graduation examination first. However, graduation certificates will be issued only after the documents have been verified and the qualifications have been reviewed. If it is found that the documents are forged or that the student's academic qualifications are insufficient, even if they pass the joint examination and graduation examination, their graduation qualifications will be revoked to show punishment and prevent opportunism. In addition to the separate order, this order is hereby issued for compliance.

Jiangxi Senior Vocational School Enrolling Transfer Students During Winter Break 277

The Jiangxi Senior Vocational School and Jiangxi Junior High School, founded by Mr. Li Liejun and Mr. Zhang Dingfan, although only open for a few months, have quite complete facilities. The teaching hours range from 45 hours per week for the most, and no less than 42 hours for the least, with special emphasis on physical education. There are morning and evening exercises every day without interruption. Even on Saturday afternoons, classes are still held as usual. Self-study is especially strict. Students get up at 5:30 every morning to work and are not allowed to return to the dormitory until after the 9:30 pm self-study session. During rest periods, they play games on the sports field or review their lessons in the self-study room. The self-study room is divided into senior vocational and junior high sections, both supervised by teachers on duty. Even on Sundays, students must obtain a leave pass from the Dean of Students before leaving the school. Female students are not allowed to ask for leave unless they have a personal letter of verification from their parents. At the same time, the school has organized clubs, including music, drama, martial arts, and chess groups. During regular weekly holidays, teachers and students gather happily, which not only prevents idleness and fosters physical and mental well-being, but is also a distinctive feature of the school's moral education. The school also pays extraordinary attention to hygiene, with a hygiene committee within the school, in which all students participate. They take turns managing cleaning, epidemic prevention, and inspecting kitchen meals every day, and hold a major cleaning session every week. Students are not allowed to have any other outside expenses except for laundry and haircuts. The school fees are also extremely low, with each person spending no more than 100 yuan per semester, including all expenses. It is said that the school's business, civil engineering materials, general studies, and junior high school classes still have dozens of vacancies, and they plan to enroll transfer students during the winter break.
